O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	You, three sons, I have fulfilled this book that is behind the science of medicine, the fulfillment of it, and made the end through its exposures and by its declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to my vision that I have fulfilled this book with this surgery, which is part of the work of hands, it is to say "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is forbidden in our region and is rejected in every way, if it is perceived by science and knowledge, and there is nothing more to do than the small descriptions in books that the hands have moved.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And this has led to the error and vanities, and the intentions are closed and science is alienated.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	I seem that I could revive it by assembling the order of this treatment according to the way of exposure and declaration and abbreviation.
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	and I will come together the forms of firebrands of cauterization and other tools of the work with the assembly of the declaration and preparation of it, as he is skilled.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And because no one of the hands masters is found in our hands, the art of medicine is extended.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And it is necessary for him who enters the science of anatomy, as Galen says, to know the judgment of the members, and their forms and conjunctions and separations of the parts, and to have knowledge of the bones, the nerves, the muscles and the number of joints, and the movement and rest of the limbs, and the issue of the same.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	And because Ypocras says that with the non it is not made, and with the work it is few.
et meismement en l’art de main.	and likewise in the art of hand.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	We say in the introduction of this book that who is not acquainted with things before said, if he will make it without error and not deceive the men.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	I have many times wanted to write about these who come into this science and if they abandon this science and sense experiment.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	I see a madman who cuts off the scrotum of a woman and cuts the collateral arteries of her neck.
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	because so much blood flows out that the woman dies in her hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	And I see another madman who treats a piercing of an old man and the piercing was large.
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	if he carried with him a piece of the bladder, and he died the enemy in three years.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	I had not yet been called to treat this wound, and I saw the position of the patient and the size of the wound, and if it was not cut well, he died.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	And I see another madman who cured the duke of our land who had a broken leg and with the fracture there was pain.
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	And the patient's ignorance tightens the wound on the wound as it has been done by a strong time, and does not leave any pain in the wound, and leaves it in its final state.
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	and he commands that it should not be loosened.
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	and waited until the leg was all swollen and the foot came to destruction.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	I am called upon to come to him, and I hurried to free the leg.
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	and when I loosened it, it was in pain but did not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	But all the paths of his corruption were already confirmed or member, and it could not be cured.
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	And the corruption spreads to the arm as long as the limb is completely wasted.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And see another reason why it will fall and be enchanted, and then burned by the malice of his lordship.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For chancre, when it is free of melancholic matter, only one thing can be done if it is not in its entirety the part that can be completely cured of what is corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	And for this reason, dear children, you should know that the work of hands is divided into two parts:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	it is to know whether it is safe or if there is more risk in other positions.
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	and I will show in each case of this book where there is fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	And it is important that you keep this in mind, so that the foolish may not speak ill of you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	If you take your weapons in hand, and your physicians lightly but firmly, and use the best method if by God's grace you come to health and be strong.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	Et leave the terrible diseases of grief in health.
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	And put your weapons aside because of what you doubt, and be sure in yourself that you can come from this world to the other with glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	Galen's advice is given in no uncertain terms.
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	Do not take medicine for illness without first consulting a wise physician.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have heard this treatise is discussed in three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	The first chapters are about fire cautery and medical cauterization, and this is the ordered chapter for the physician up to the point.
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	and of the forms of stitches, and of the forceps for cauterization, and of everything that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	The second chapter is about cutting and perforating, and ventouses and wounds, and the extraction of arrows, and similar things.
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	and order the chapters and the forms of the stitches.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and torsions, and similar things.
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	and it is ordered of the loosening of the joints and the forms of stitches.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	However, if we remember our work, it is necessary that I give the quality of the aid and no less for each complexity.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	I say that the quality of aid, and not harm, is the longest speech and the most subtle science and the secret remedy.
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	And many spoke of the arrows, and they agreed to this.
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	And they speak a little of their words, for I question their age.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	I say that burning helps universally with all complexions or matter, however, the complexion:
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	It is to know that hot complexion has matter, and dry complexion has matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	In hot and dry complexions, they all have matter, and they say that burning is great help;
et li autre dirent le contraire:	and the other says the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	that burning is not good for disease that comes from choler and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	For the nature of hot fire is hot, and should not be curative for hot disease by choler, nor by dryness;
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	And then comes the one who says that cauterization does not help with the disease of heat and dryness that comes into the hearts of men.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	For when you perceive the chest of the patient and its moisture on the complexion of fire, you must quickly close the chest.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this word.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have never found it once by experience.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	And all ways should be avoided as much as possible by him who has experienced it and knows the chapter of cauterization, and the diversity of complexions of men, and their dispositions and causes of their diseases, and their symptoms and the spaciousness of tens.
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	of other complexions we have no cause, just as in cold and damp diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And then they are supposed to fit together and agree with the cauterization.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	Understand, children, that cauterization is a fire if it contains secrets of healing, and even more beneficial than fire medicine.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For the fire is simple, and only comes to harm to the member it is cooked in, and does not hurt other members.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	The hot medicines come from one part of the body to another by moving them, and they bring diseases of grief to the healthy condition.
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	And by chance, the patient was caught.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	I had it for its height and for the goodness of its substance, which does not do harm, if it has no excess.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	And I found it through experiment and the length of service and study I have given to this art, and it is true in things.
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	and because I apologize for the length of my speech, as I only like to tell you the secret that is contained in fire or water, and the quality of the work, as it affects the diseases of the body, just as the philosopher says when demonstrating.
or le recevez en vos pensees.	1. For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	1. Know, son, that the burns should be made in certain ways and not too tightly.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	I say that cauterization is useful in all cases, because the wounds are not properly cared for by the help of cauterization.
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	And I say that cauterization is useful for necessary pain and haste, which cannot be waited by the greatest malice that comes to the member.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	And do not think less, dear fellow, if they follow the example of the master.
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	For the disease that is cured by cauterization has no return.
et il le dient ensi;	and he says thus.
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	but it is not so with everyone because cauterization is only a medicine that dries the complexion, and drys the humors that cause pain, and is worth more than other medicines for hastening the courage, and for the virtue of his work and his nobility.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	And it is possible that the disease grows once according to the complexion of the patient and the strength of the disease and its virtue.
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	And the surplus is acquired by the acquisition of meat and similar things, if not cauterized, it is administered to the patient or they have little surplus and moisture, just like cauterization for toothache, and the similar things, and part of the pain does not return.
mais ce avient poc.	But this is rare.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	And many people do not understand that cauterization is called the end of medicine, and this is true.
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	But they only believe that cauterization is useless after medicine, but they understand it to be false, and it is cauterization of medicine because when we have means of treating any disease in no way they are effective, therefore we administer our cauterization and it is useful.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	However, it is well understood that cauterization is part of medicine, even if some do not agree with this.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	The ancients said that cauterization of instruments of gold was as deadly as of iron, and they did not say this because of the quality of the gold and the highness of its substance.
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	and they said that cauterization of the lees does not make any difference, but this is not true because I have experienced it and found that it is true in some men.
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	For the golden cautery, it is worth as much as iron, if they say so.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	And you know when you are heating an instrument of gold, you do not feel it when it is heated by the color of gold, and it has cooled down the most.
et s’on le chaufe trop;	And if you heat it too much.
si font au feu;	If they put it in the fire.
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	and it has enough prevention.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And that's why we use fire cauterization in our work because we have already used it.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or if you have ordered this chapter of the small joints, because it is easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	oil cauterization
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	oil cauterization is useful for moisture and cold in the eye socket, and when it is caused by a disease called "soda", and by many humors that descend to the small joints as the ears, and the ears, and by numerous sleeps and tooth pain and throat pain, and even by all diseases that come from cold, such as paralysis, apoplexy, and semblances of diseases.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	The form of this cautery is that if the patient is purged by medicine soluble modifying the throat III or IV, according to which virtue and courage and accustomation of the patient he can bear it.
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	And then do the head of the patient again.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	Then place the patient's head between your hands, and put your hands on either side of it.
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	After, place the root of your palm on the root of his nail between his two fingers.
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	And if your two fingers come together, it will bleed, and then wash the fire cautery which is called "olivare", which is in this form:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	And place it on the thumb's signet of ink, and then slowly and gently pull down and stretch your hand a little at a time, and gently.
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	Then gently relax your hand, and reward the nail if you see the first bone is very small.
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	and if you do not see it, if the cauterization resumes as soon as you see the bone, like I told you.
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	after taking hold of the needle, and putting on some soft cotton, and placing it on the leg, and leaving it for three days.
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	after sewing with a fine thread.
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	and leave it until the burn is completely healed.
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	after treating the wound with the ointment called "tetrafarmacone", until it is healthy.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	And tell him that as the wound becomes older, it purges more.
et por ce si aide mues.	And for this reason, assistance is needed.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And none of these say that too much fatigue is needed for the cauterization, but rather part of the bone should be burned, and then what is burned is removed, and it is treated.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	And the other is that one should shave as long as possible, and then stick it as hard as possible into the bone until it is as wide as the woman's vulva, because the humors flow out.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	And one should shave the overgrown wound long.
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	After that, it should be cured and soothed.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	And these two methods of cauterization do not seem to be the best in any way, since in no man has it been found that there is fear.
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	And I think that I should leave it alone.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	And similarly when the head of the shoulder is weak by nature, and the first appearance of cauterization is more gentle and painless for me, and I therefore use it in order to assemble salute.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	1. of the ancient pain of the head
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	When the entire shoulder comes with chronic pain, and lasts for a long time, if it must use herbs and pills called "cochie", and purification of the shoulder and oils and plasters;
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	And when you make the cauterization that we have mentioned before, it does not work.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	The head of the shoulder is dislocated when the patient is very sick and it is not too tight.
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	Therefore, the fire cautery should be used on that part as we have previously described.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	After the fire cautery is applied to each corner of the shoulder joint as we have previously described, and then the fire cautery is applied to the part that is called "thongs".
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	and they are held in place with ventouses.
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	and hold your hand tight if you do not see the bone.
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	The patient feels much greater pain in this cautery than in others, and I will speak to you later.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	and it is necessary that the burns on the corners be more sensitive than those made on the child's head, and this is the form:
dou cautere dou chief	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	When there is sudden pain in the head of the child, and it spreads throughout the body, and the head is purged with medicines, and the other treatments I have mentioned in the division of diseases are made, but none of them benefit much.
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	Therefore, I make the burns in two ways, that is to say, with medicinal herbs and with iron.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	The burn made with medicinal herbs is if you take a dose of alum, and it helps to remove the scar and the rupture, and then they make the temple where the pain is held in a way that you can put the dose of alum back on the skin.
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	And when it is reset, if the limb is held well and left alone for twelve hours.
et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III;	Then remove the bandage and apply a poultice of oak gall, leaving it on for two to three days.
puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	Then dip your finger in vinegar as much as possible and press the wound.

se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	if you see, if it is pointed at the head to one and another, and if you see, if it is as a tent.
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	but this which is twisted is useful for your work.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	After pressing the fistula it will be flattened, and in the gristle, and it is dried.
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	and it is closed if the hand, and the gristle becomes the belly.
aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie;	After placing the hot iron, and hold your hand on the iron at the edge where it meets the oil, so your hands do not burn.
et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	and place the iron in the oil grease, and it will become corrupted.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the beginning of the fire cautery on the bone, it would be good.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors;	If not, then relight the iron again, and if you manage to do it, and let it cool for three hours.
aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers;	After that, put cotton on the wound and apply a drying ointment as soon as it is clean, and let it pass ten days without it being clean, if you apply an acidic corrosive medicine as soon as the bone is exposed.
et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	And so he follows what comes in his chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And there is a way of cauterization of fistulas that no of the ancients said.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu;	Understand the fistula, and then the knee;
aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	Afterward, put in the fenestra, and there is a subtle change in this form:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc;	and they make it to the quantity of an .Z. of plunk;
et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil;	and hold your hand firmly on the fenestra, and do not move the patient at all, until the plunk is firmly set in its place;
et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe:	and it is necessary to put on the oil with soft cotton wool in the corner of the eye or in the eyelid;
li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	The plunk if it is art to the knee of the fistula, and the health of the saffron is saved;
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	If the fistula is healed by the fire cautery we have described, that is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, then it is necessary to administer physick to the umbilicus, and to bring the fistula back to its proper place according to what is appropriate for the patient's own belly.
des crevaices en levres	cracks in the lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Many times cracks in the lips are called "cracks" and also in the lips of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these cracks as we have described in divisions, and the cure does not help, then use a small fire cautery according to this form:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font;	And he puts it in those cavities as soon as they arrive.
aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	After curing the wound so that it is healthy.
de l’aposteme de la goule	Of the abscess of the groin
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule;	When abscess comes from the root of the gall or in the uterus, or from the teeth, after taking and lying down and it becomes inflamed and turns into a fistula.
et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie:	And you cure it as we have said in divisions, and it does not benefit at all.
adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule;	Therefore, you must use the cautery according to the size of the fistula.
aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu;	After the bore or puncture of the fistula, and hold your hand until the wound is closed from the inside, and if it bleeds.
et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And I make once or twice, after we have cured what we have said in the cures, as long as it is healthy.
et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin;	And if it is cured once or twice, it is good.
et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	And if not, then you must expose the bone and expose the corrupt bone, according to what you will find in this chapter.
dou movement des dens	The first line of the translated text is "For the fire

aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent;	After shaving the cauterant whose form came here in this way, as you put a collar around the tooth.
et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent;	And he puts the fire cautery on the wound, and holds his hand so tightly that the patient feels pain coming from the root of the tooth.

de la dolor des dens	of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	When pain in the teeth comes due to cold, or it is cold, or visible, and the treatment of medicine does not help, then it is necessary to know how to perform the fire cautery in two ways.
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	and fire cautery and fire cautery.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	Fire cautery, if they are such that you burn wool, and the end in a iron or copper cup.
aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez;	After taking cotton and wrapping it around the tip of a pin, and building a flame with wool, and then placing the tooth on it gently and holding it until it cools down.
et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	And I often do so until the virtue reaches the root of the tooth, and if you see that the wool and cotton are burning, and place the tooth on it, and then put a piece of iron as hot as possible at the end of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	The first line of the text translates to: "If the fire cauterization is such that it burns several hairs of iron or gold, and it is large so that the fire does not reach the mouth of the patient.
aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez;	After heating the cauterization, if it forms a certain way, and places it on the tooth, and holds your hand until the cauterization is cooled down.
fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	Do this often, as the pain will be less for you or the next day.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer;	And it is necessary that the patient fills his mouth with hot butter in the pressure of this cauterization, and then it becomes red.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	It is the form of the fire cautery:

des scrophules	The first sentence to translate is "des scrophules
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie;	When the scrophules are soft and cold, and do not obey digestion by medicines, therefore wash the fire cautery blade after coming to its form, and it has openings for the smoke to issue from the other side;

de la toust	Of the whole

de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.

And if it is dislocated, something comes out quickly, therefore a cautery is made on the thick part of the cautery clamp, or rather, the point where cauterization is pricked.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	For the joint is closed, and the moisture is removed, and the pain is eased.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When coldness and moisture come to the stomach, and they are drawn out of it as soon as possible, and the purges are given to it, and according to customary cures, but it does not improve, then it is necessary that the patient's back be soaked with water, and his legs and hands are extended.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture;	For this, after the third cautery, I cut off the clavicle at the place where the amount of one is equal to the number of cauteries, and I divide the costals as much as the appearance of the cauteries is at three angles, and there should be space between them so that they do not become united as they grow;
et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	And may the cautery be used if they touch the two parts of the ear, and the figure of the cautery should be according to this form and not be too large or small.

Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the cure we had before, as long as it is healthy.

dou cautere de pleuresin	Therefore, it is not possible to overcome it, and I believe it is better
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere:	The ancients said that one should make of burns with roots of Aristolochia, and in the same way:

de ydropisie	The first sentence to translate is "de ydropisie
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not for dropsy, but in the way that is called "ascites.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you cure according to the methods we have described in divisions, and your cure does not benefit, then it is necessary that you make four cauterizations around the bowels, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the kidneys, and two at the back of the spine, and one at the end of the penis;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	And let the cauterization be well near the edge of the ear.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After the cauterization, let the patient lie down with their hair wet, and do not delay the treatment of the patient after the cauterization.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	And the healing will be faster, and the two intentions will be assembled with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cauterization is on the abdomen, it is the clavicle that we have before to show it.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	And on the back, it is olive-colored, according to what is placed in front of it.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the wrapping of the arrows
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are wrinkled and are like amber, and they are flat, it is necessary to cauterize on the back of the foot between the ear and the anus.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	And gently place your hand with the cauterization so as not to return.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too much in front, otherwise it may be too rough for the awl, and let the fire cautery be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After, make two cauterizations on each leg at the sharp point of the nail.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the longer cauterization be on the outside of the thigh, in front, and the other on the inside of the leg.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauterizations long enough to cure, as they are in their place.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after the cure of the other cures that we have spoken of.
de la menoison	of the menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When the abdomen comes from cold and moisture, as long as the vitamins and digestive substances that are in the stomach and intestines are affected and cannot be cured by usual methods,
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	When you see the patient in great pain and with great courage, if they have had a cauterization on the stomach according to what they have spoken of before or a cauterization on the stomach, the cauterization circulates.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	And four cauterizations are made on the anus at all the fine cauterization wires, and two cauterizations are made on the thighs.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the patient suffering, then perform the cauterization on the point, and the cauterization on each side, and the punctures in the stomach, for the cure is beneficial when it has good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure of the hemorrhages
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the embolisms are either formed or formed at the base, and they are old and consist of large cold and moist humors that are corrupted, and they are treated as we have described in divisions, and there is no benefit if a cauterization is made:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	In the third line, they suspend the spine of the other side, which is completely bare and unevenly cut, and then perform the fire cautery on the buttock twice.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	And if you think that his stomach is cold and the meat is not cooked, and the face starts to bulge, then the face on which the fire cautery was performed as previously mentioned, and the other on the liver, and the other on the gallbladder at all the cautery clavicle.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	And leave the fire cautery long enough.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the wound is healed, it will be healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the charnosite which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut the wound, if the fire cautery appears to be too sharp, then put it completely on fire and then place it all burning on the wound.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and it leaves so much of your hand that the cauterization does not reach the birth of the vein, because it is not cut.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if it does not come out, then cauterize each time as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the treatment of wounds, using them as much as they are healthy.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large cauterization on the skin, it will give more help.
de plaie mal curee	A wound that has not been properly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure tightness or opening, we will tell you about it in their own words, if they come to a serious illness that cannot be cured by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no fistula, and it is awake and gushes pus and corrupt moisture, if you provide total care to the wound, and keep the patient aware of the entire wound as much as possible.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After rinsing the cauterization that seems to be a rasor, and remove it through the fistula according to the amount that tries and is entered, and resume the cauterization as long as the corset is porris and corrupted, once, or twice, depending on the amount of the tumor.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	And take care of the wounds of the nerves that are injured, and the large wounds.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	If the fistula is at the course of the uterus and the intestine, and you treat these wounds, and do not use any other means than leeches, and think that it is not serious, then.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	After treating the wound until it is healthy, and if the wound is clean, and the materials are long and strong, then you can be sure that the wound is completely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	And if the materials are not long and strong, it is certain that the wound is not healed, and the bone at the end is affected.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	And as for one of these that we will tell in his arm.
de la maladie des reins	Of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain in the head comes on, and large ventosity, and no woman can bear it, then it is necessary that you cauterize him on both sides of the head with the cautery clavicle that we have mentioned before.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	And if we cauterize him in the environment, then there will be three cauterizations in line, and they will give more aid.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is full and weak from headache and moisture, if the patient retains urine, then you should cauterize on the part opposite the bladder, where the hair grows at the opening, both on the left and right sides, and each one should be cauterized like a penis.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	And you make the fire cautery on the back, or it will give you pain.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	And the cautery stick should be made according to the form mentioned before.
de la marris	Of the marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the matrix is cold and moist, and does not allow for the formation of semen, and the flowers are rotten and their ends delayed.
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	And when they come, it causes great pain.
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	Therefore, it is necessary to cut the third cauterization through the belly, as we have said or cutting from the bladder, and it causes pain on the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	And the cautery stick should be made according to what we have said.
de la hainche	Of the hedgehog
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the moisture-like substances descend to the handle of the axe, and for this reason if it remains motionless in its sheath, then the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together.
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and if it is found that the thigh is in the wrong department, then you must cauterize the patient's shoulder on the axe handle in the manner of a circle, and hold the shoulder before the axe as it turns, so that the axe is outside the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if it is done in such a way that it resembles the cauterization of the stomach;
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if such cauterization is not present, then make three olive-sized cauterizations on the patient's thigh, and let them be as similar as possible to all the others;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and the treatment as long as it is healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	for the pain of the shoulder
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes in the shoulder bone, and it is cold and moist, and the patient is treated as we have described in the division, and the treatment is not effective, and the disease is old.
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	therefore it is necessary that you purge the patient of large humors with fetid pills or other bone-like pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After I have done the cauterization;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the way to cauterize is done in two ways:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	it is necessary to know how to assemble burning drugs and cauterize with fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	If the fire cautery is performed in various ways, some of them are like this:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	If you cauterize the horse's hoof, do it in this way: third, make a triangular cauterization according to this form, and have good depth and breadth, and leave between each cauterization the size of a thumb, and it will be olive-colored;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Never has it been done to cauterize on the neck of the horse's hoof, because there are four ways according to this form;
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see, if you cauterize at the circle we mentioned before in the displacement of the horse's hoof;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	But I make it in such a way that the circles contain all the hair, and all the sharp points are cut.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in sciatica, when the pain holds in the buttock and does not reach the thigh or the knee.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And when it comes to the thigh and leg, if the pain is severe as the surgeon says, I cauterize there at the ankle, IV times, on the left side, a small piece.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	And if it is the cauterizing kind, and the sharp points are many.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if the surgeon feels that the pain extends to two or more points or near the enquiry, then he should cauterize at the point where he feels the pain, either three or four in the cauterization which is called "points.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if it is skilled, then I will do more.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is from the groin to the thigh, then it should be cauterized with a cauterizing iron or a circular cauterizing instrument. And you should take good care of all your cauterizations so that you do not cause further harm and damage to the nerves and large arteries, and so that you do not cause more pain and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen more cases where cautery was done on the ankle, and they hurt so much that the entire leg became inflamed, and the toe as well, and it was noticed and corrupted in all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a solution of belly which he lost his life.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts assembled, make a fire cautery on both sides according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise ones said in the cauterization of the thigh, whether it is this way or that, I will do it in such a way and so large as to be as big as some nail's head or a smaller one, and it should be intertwined and interwoven, and should be spaced out and spaced apart, according to the quantity of a new nail's head.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and be between the intercostal muscles of the second part, and also like bones, and if it has a good piece of iron.
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form.
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And wash it as much as it is red and gritty, and then put it on the mallet of the malaise hail, and be twisted around the sharp chest.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and the cauterization is once the cautery is made and left for three days.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then apply a plaster of burr, and leave the wound open long ten.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment of ointment as it is healthy.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasim says that we use very little of this cauterization due to its harshness, and few people use it.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and all that is harsh cauterization, which can be endured, and later it does not matter.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	If the ardent cauterization is that you make and an instrument with interlocks in the corner of the door, and it is either of iron or of steel, and in the high part has us, and between each the quantity of the growth of a tooth.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and be overwhelmed and connected, and they are joined together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After placing the handle of the axe on the patient's shoulder, which is firmly grasped, and pressing your hand firmly against the handle of the axe.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After heating the hot water in the pot and leaving it for an hour, the patient suffers from the pain and inflammation of the wound.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it also has the effect of burning as if by fire.
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And when the mordication has passed, take your hand with the instrument and gently lift the handle of the axe, leaving it for three days, and then cover it with as much as the black part of the eschar is healed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	And let it remain for three days without food or drink;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and that would be the assistance from the side after the treatment of wounds as soon as it is healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, make an instrument that burns according to what you have done in the shoulder.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And this is the way of the hot iron, and I have written or treated about the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkaline and live charcoal, as much of one as the other, mix them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	or there is a small hole that can be pointed with a razor and entered.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place on it another and better one, and place some alkaline and salt and soft ash on it, until you have made as many powders as you will have in your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	And he leaves it as is until the water comes down with the ague and chill, then takes all of this water, and mixes it with chalk and alkaline soap as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And when it will be in the heat and is maintained in the mouth of medicines and in cauteries of other members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it makes the work like fire, and if other medicines are used well, such as burning the heel with honey and anacardic acid and chalk with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	Galiens tells us of a remedy by which some were cured of the pain in the thigh and sciatica, and he said that no other remedy was needed, and that it was cured in one time after this remedy, and he was bathed as he instructs afterwards.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And then in this way that you prescribe green leaves with fresh and dry verdure, and the mouth is greased with a little fat, and it is placed on the heel, the thigh, and the leg where the pain is, and it is tied.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	When left alone for three hours, the patient no longer feels the pain.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	Then I make him enter a bath as long as the chest is raised, and then I let him enter a cold bath, and the pain will all leave and he will be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And you advise that no one should use such cauterizing medicines after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	Dyascorides says that if the sciatic nerve is cauterized with goat's hair, it helps to relieve the pain.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And it should be made in a particular way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the mustard and beat it with oil, and put it in the hole that is between the thumb and the other which is called the fossil.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After drying the goat hair, and burning it until it is charred, and then putting it on the hair, and leaving it as long as it remains stained.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	And repeat the process again, and continue doing it as long as you feel by touch that it is returning to its place, and that the pain is ceasing.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	And these methods of cauterization are called "goat's cauterization".
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain in the back of the neck
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back of the neck, whether from scratching or percussion or from too much evacuation, or from the appearance of expanded cold matter, none of these appearances is worth cauterization, rather it is for that which comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	After the patient is free from drugs or other substances, and they are lying on their back, if the pain persists, three lines of incisions should be made, and in each line, cauterize or more according to the will and ability of the patient.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	And it should be done with the cauterization according to the one called "points".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	And if you see, make three or four cauterizations at the clavicle mole according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This disease often affects many children, and the signs of the beginning are that they strangle when they start to grow, and cry.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you push on the back of the spine and on the appearance that comes with the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you see it heal, if the cauterization is done on the cauterizing tool according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cauterization becomes brown in every part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, if the cauterization is done at the end of the spine with the cauterizing tool touching the second or third line and they are points close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After healing the limb to the extent that it is healthy according to what we have said, and you are warned that you will not perform a fire cauterization on the gilbositeit which is in the spame of the nerf.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When pain in the joints due to moisture is expanded to each member of the body, and when pain comes in the foot, which they call "gout" properly, and when it is of cold cause and remedies by medicines do not cure it, it is cured by cauterization in a certain way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	make the cut of cauterization at the end of the joint, and the olive-oil cauterization in this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	If he thinks that you prick at the cheek, then he orders a burn to be performed on the entire area claimed as "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	When the pain comes to the knee and other joints, and this happens often, I would cauterize on each knee three times or four times on each part, using olive oil.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you have more skill, but do not hold your hand for as long as it takes to see the effect,
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	If the pain descends to the jaw and back, then he administers the cauterization we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pain is in the hands, then make points every two lines.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	And if there is no more pain, then make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pain comes to the wrists or spines, then cauterize each part and give the patient government to the midwife and medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you make the patient govern with medicines and purge the blood, then they will be cured by God.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When rupture comes in writhings, and the bones descend as strings, and it is novel, if it happens that when you see to cure it, it does not lose its juice;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that it uses things that relieve the stomach, if it descends from its stomach;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	After the wound is placed on your back between your hands, and he commands that you shave your hair until it is smooth, and cuts it with your nails, and signs of healing appear on the bone point, and there are signs that resemble half of a circle at the corners of the corners;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then rinse the cauterization with the form that is here, which is his shape;
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as it is white and has a glistening feel.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the buns on their legs;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and he shaves his hand on what it does not return;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and works well on the thighs of the patient, and puts the ointment and the salve on the thighs, and the other on the place where he shaves the hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cauterization at the sign with all your hand, and hold it right and hold it as long as you reach the bone, and if you do not reach the first time, then continue again as soon as you touch the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and be gentle with yourself so that the bile does not rise when you do the cauterization.
que tu ne le brulasses;	so that you do not burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and so that the patient does not die, or other wounds.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And you should know when you come to the bone at the cauterization, your efforts are worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cauterization of children be done gently according to the size of the part, and also for adults, according to their size.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days, cure the leg of the patient as much as possible until the burn is healed.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after the treatment of other wounds as much as possible until it is healthy, and let the patient lie on his back for 14 days on the side where the wound is painful.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary that his nails be long, so that the feces do not stick when he goes to the bathroom in private rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after 14 days, when he wants to get up, make him wear a well-made girdle, and every other day.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and take plenty of rest, work hard and do not drink too much beer and wine, and do not snore too much.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And when this teaching is made, it is entirely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after the cutting in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When routs (hernias) come to other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow any more, the fire cautery is applied again according to its quantity, and it should be done in three places.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	After the treatment according to what we have said.
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And no of the ancients have said that it should be done at the fire cautery at three angles according to this form.
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	1. The shoulder rises and I make a line for the width of the fracture, and another for the defense, and hold the patient's hand at all the cauterization point.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	2. But the first cauterizations are more gentle and milder.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	3. there is no pain in any limb.
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	4. When pain comes in any limb, whether from cold or injury, and this pain persists for a long time, and medicine does not help, then it is necessary to cauterize at the point called "points", and to cauterize according to the length of the limb, its thickness, its weakness, its location of torsions and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If it is healthy for the first fire cautery, that is well.
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If this is the case, continue with another fire cautery on it, for custom is that one must die in the member that is proximate, because it comes to the fire cauteries as long as the pain is healthy.
de meselerie	of medicine
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The remedies are never helpful once through cauterization, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of flesh and melancholy.
