et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	And may the heads of the two bones at the two ends of the incision be set in place, and may they be shaped so that when they are assembled, it will resemble the figure of a letter that does not have "I griesche".
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	Then, that char, according to the amount of its cost, which is greater than the paper, then adjust the two uneven parts, and the cost of a linen thread.
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, for the cures we have mentioned for mollifying medicines and tents, as long as they are healthy.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the disease comes from a cut or a wound or a cauterization, then it is necessary that you make a flat cut of the hair of the paper according to what is before.
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	Then describe between the two shoulders of a tent, as I said.
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	And you must make the incision according to the shape of the disease, as it varies in shape, and the skilled masters can adjust everything to return it to its natural form.
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	And the patient himself, according to what is needed for the incision and excision in various positions.
dou soudement de la papiere	I would shave off the paper.
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this suture is made by women in a certain way that the paper of it is soaked with white oil, and cannot move or make its natural cuts, then it is necessary that you touch the end of a razor with the wet paper, and hold it up;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	and the stitches are removed as long as you cover what is inserted in the subcutaneous layer, which is not too thick nor too thin, so that the patient does not suffer from the subcutaneous layer too much nor has the oil leaked out.
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and make sure your incision, which you scrape of the one assembled, lightly, so that the paper re-forms according to its natural shape.
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and it becomes healthy all that assembled, and never in the oil salty water, and raise it with sweet water, and with warmth.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	Then put between the paper and the oil a tent of linen, and put on the oil smooth hair in a lot of glue.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	And afterwards, after the third day, use a warm poultice and things that are damp until it is healthy again.
de l’ungle de l’oil	Of the finger of the oil
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	There are two ways to cut the nail:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	It is nervous and resembles hard sandstone, and another that is not nervous but resembles dry moisture frozen, which when touched with fire and cooked with tongs, if it cannot be done;
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	and the other one resembles towards the great lurker, and grows little by little until it covers all the vision and all the light and the movement of the oil.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the manner of the incision is that the surgeon places his finger in the wound, then he cuts the hairs.
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	And soften the paper with your hand, then pick up the pincher with a small opening, and hold it at the end.
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	Then take a needle, and insert a horsehair, or sheephair, or beaverhair, and a strong thread.
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	Then double the point of the needle with your finger, and pull the thread through the needle, and perforate all the needle, and tie it with one thread and hold it at the end, and scrape off all the hair from the edge of the needle that touches the prunele and the silk at the tip of the chief, then cut off the remaining in the root of the armor as subtle as possible and as small forces as possible, and leave the natural or alloyed char, so that by the incision does not come the corps of the tears habitually.
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	and no time has it been set in its place solely, and as for that, as we have said.
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	Then the scorching, we have all the substance of it, and the form is like this:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And be careful that the substance does not touch the chipped tile and break it, and the pruning does not occur.
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	and then after the incision, a little oil is put into the wound, and dough is made from litargire, and it is left until the next day.
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the treatment of that which is to be done until it is healthy.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the finger is not very nervous, and you do not push the needle, and the joints cannot enter, this appearance of a finger of medicines is often treated many times.
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and I have told you in the division, and if you see it covered, if you work the oil of the woman, and take the light spumous substance according to this form:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And dip the finger subtly, and if you see that it does not become soft and the reason is pressed, if you distill from your mouth the oil of colchicum made from litargire and red colchicum and seil broiet, and it stupefies the oil to the other part;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	Then continues the other evacuation according to this same work, as soon as it is all complete.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If nothing is against you in the oil, as with an abscess, then the milk, and first treat the abscess as soon as it is healthy, then continue the prick as before, as long as it is healthy.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh of the arm is dark in the oil at night due to great pain, and a part is affected but not all, that tears do not come;
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	then it distills into the oil that is redder, which is made of lividity.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the wood that was carved by the plum tree
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	The hairs of some men never turn red, and they prune them and roll them on papers and turn them into flowers, and seem like a rose of the dragon.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	And the patient, if the surgeon places his head in your hand, then he manipulates the limbs, and all that is uncomfortable and inconvenient is adjusted to this, and support is given with strength.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then adjust the first knot, and pull everything to the end, and make sure you do not cut the thread at the seam;
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	And let the incision be done with a sharp knife that we have mentioned in the incision of the toe, and with slight forces you can open it, if as the chapter shows after this chapter it is demonstrated;
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	And when the incision is completed and all the knots are open, if you use oil of silk or distilled red wine and similar corrosive medicines, and apply it with a cotton dipped in urine, so that it is sure to stop bleeding;
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	If it does not cause pain, and the flesh surrounds it, and you doubt the healing of the wound, then leave the oil and cure the healing of things that soothe the wound.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	Then return to your work as soon as it is safe, and then make several cuts in the oil by this appearance.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	But it is necessary that you soften the cure of every weak oil of the natural way.
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and from the accidental way of work, in the knife of iron.
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	and do not insert your hand into any of these works until you see that your limbs are calm in this work.
des voines des eulz	of the veins of the hairs
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	These are red veins that are covered with oil, and they touch the eye and blunt the oil for all time.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	The first sentence translates to: "However, the first thing you notice is the oil, in its state, is false, and there is no other disease than the false one.
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	However, the treatment is done in this way:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	Instruct the patient to cut their hair short and even, then let the wounds heal according to their ability, and make the wounds subtle according to this form:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en I cors selonc ceste forme:	And let there be as many as one thousand degrees in one corpse according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	Then you can reset the wounds subtly, and remove the remaining oil from the wounds as much as possible, until you see the wounds free of oil:
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	and make sure you do not weep the oil with the points of the spatula, and do this work at noon before the sun, and be as eager in your work so that you do not miss any stitches.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	and when you have finished, if you distill the green and red oil to cool what is left of the bellows.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you cannot distill all of it in that hour, then make a plaster with the oil of things that soothe the pain of the eyes, and leave some for as long as the pain is soothing and secure from gangrene, then resume according to this method until it is healthy again.
et c’est li forme des forces:	And it is the form of the forces:
de la fistule de l’oil	Of the fistula of the oil
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	It calls "arissati" fistulas:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	When you cure with fire cautery and by using hot medicine according to what I have said before, and it is not completely healed, then it must be opened, and all the moisture that is in it must be drained, as long as the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is exposed, and you will see the corruption and darkness, if all the instrument of this thing is in its form,
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	and is called "spraying," and it is made of firm wood, and it is cut like a knife if it is in the present form:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And put on the leg of the corrupted bone, then twist it between your two hands, and press your hand a little until you feel that the corruption is set.
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do this once, then restore the leg with exfoliating medicines.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the leg is swollen and hard, and the belly is also swollen, and it remains so for over XL years, and it does not heal or become infected, and no accidents occur, you should be reassured that it is healthy.
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	If not, then there is no other way but to bring the fistula back to the affected area according to this form:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	When the first dislocation occurs, it is necessary to realign the bone the second time using force and medicines called "agues," and if the patient feels pain according to this form, then the head of the shoulder should be fixed at three angles, and the force applied should be gentle as much as possible, just like you see here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	Then place the shoulder bone on the arm, and gently pull your hand away from the oil, then turn the entire forearm so that it pierces the bone and feels it through the flesh as if you are holding your hand on your neck;
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	And then restore the dry medicines as I have shown you, and when it is cooked and hardened, if it sticks to the neck, then it is the material for the shoulder;
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	If there is a lighter thing on the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	of the oil's end
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the wound is fully open and there is no sign of obstruction or inflammation in the urine, then you must examine the patient.
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	Then the nurse should perform a urinalysis using a sterile tube, without causing any harm. Then she should mix the urine with equal parts of oil and aloe vera, and incense and sarcolic acid, and then strain the mixture, and apply it to the belts and sheets.
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	And how the sheets are applied if you have enough sheets, double each one by four, and then place them on top of each other according to the amount that the wound has.
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	Then the strain forms due to the pressure of a hard bandage, and the ventouses resume sucking without feeling pain.
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	Then the ventouses are used and left on the strained part overnight, and if the strings loosen, then you must pull it tighter.
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	Then the string after the day and night, and if you see the oil repaired, it's done.
se ce non;	If not.
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the burn returns and the cloths, the string, and the ventouses as long as it is healthy.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	Great disturbance of the eyeball
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When disruptions come in the eyelid, then it opens and comes out paper as small as a grain of resin, and it is difficult to see.
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	When you see this, the treatment is such that you insert an awl at the root of the part where the joint is dislocated, then insert another awl or a double-edged knife into the part of the arm that is injured.
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	And then, using the first awl according to the position, leave the other awl alone.
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	Then, using the double-edged knife on the other part of the arm, draw out a piece of the urethra well, then remove the awl and place some soft oil on the wound.
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	And leave it as long as the edges of the urethra heal with the urethra, then treat the oil with things that are comfortable until the wound is healed.
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	For no time is the wound restrained by any part of a circle of cloth, as long as it is healthy.

puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the hair is drawn as soon as it is healthy.
de la bowe de l’oil	from the oil's bowl
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease called "alcunnati" is not more than a bow that is assembled in the oil, resembling sharp descending, and it is not sharp.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	And the manner of appearance of the wound is that if you choose to sit the patient on the side and straight, then take the head between your two hands, and hold it as long as you see the bone coming to the end of your fingers.
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	Then tighten it, and do not let it descend and make it untangled, and see the patient's things as he alone does.
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	And if it does not descend, be sure it is inflamed, and if the bone comes out of the wound, it is not straight as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	If you sit the patient on your hands, then take the scalpel subtly and cut along the corneal edge I pot through the continuation of the conjunctive with the cornea and the corneal bulb as long as the bone is in.
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	When it comes out, if it is distilled in the hot warm oil mixed with honey, or hot or fenugreek is boiled and honey, then it is treated with another treatment until it is healthy.
des aigues de l’oil	of the cold water
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have the appearances of waters in the division, and what must be done to perceive.
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	if according to the health it is.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	It is necessary that you hold the patient between your hands as firmly as possible, being in the light of the sun, and with the healthy and narrow oil.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	Then place the paper of the oil in your left hand where the hairs are sparse, or in your right hand where the hairs are dense.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	Then take in your right hand, the hairs that are longest, the instrument called "almagda", or in your left hand, the hairs that are shortest.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	Then place the tip of the instrument at the corona through the largest part of the hole in the oil bag at the least painful point of the arm, then use the instrument called "almagda" gently, and pull your hand as much as it pierces the oil bag, and feel that almagda enters the empty space.
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	And it is necessary that the measure of the almagda hole is at the end of the spice which is just above the prickle of the nail.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	and that is the head of the shoulder
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	if you see the bone in that paper by the clarity of the corneal layer, and then place the instrument just where it is, then press on one way after another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If the patient feels faint now, if they see the surgeon in front of them and the instrument before them.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	after resting the small piece, and if the wound re-emerges on the second way, place the forceps with the instrument, and when it is secure and does not move, lightly twist your hand around a little bit.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	and then place the wound with a piece of gummy thread, and lift some oil from it.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then pour the oil into the wound, either coarse or finely ground in oil and a large amount of oil, and mix it with the healthy oil.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	Yes, and those who are ours, put on cloths with a large amount of oil.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the stone cannot enter the kidney through its hardness, because it has too many sharp hairs, then you must use the instrument called "alberit" which is in this form:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And only pierce the conjuncture, and do not push too hard, but make a small incision first, then pull out the arrowhead, as we have said.
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	And at the completion of the work, the patient feels pain in the shoulder, if it is dark in the leu.
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	And perform all movements, eat light foods, and do not move the head to the left or right, and adjust according to his natural position.
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	Then the patient stays in this house for a while, rests his eyes, and then shows me some things, and then he puts on his clothes according to the ninth hour.
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	1. and only that you do this in the care or after the incision now, but it is necessary that you align it, because the swelling increases rapidly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	1. If abscesses occur, you must slide the oil in front of the ninth day, and address the one that relieves the abscess.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	1. And when it is calmed, remove the eye and place it in a safe place for any day, and remain there in that dark house.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	1. And then exit from the house little by little, and adapt to its case.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	1. and be aware that no disciples should undergo this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	A group of people came from the Yrach region, informing us that in some areas it was practiced for centuries, but we have not seen any evidence of this in our land, nor have we ever read about it in ancient books.
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	By chance, it is a new thing.

de la char sor le neis	And of the char for the head.
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	None are born or become different wounds, but there are some that seem to have scorpion's stings at their edges.
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	If it has such things or if there is an enhancement of color from flux, and if the color is good.

puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	Then hold the forehead that comes from the pillow with one hand, and the other forehead that comes from the mouth with the other hand, and wipe it after the other in order to clean it as we do with our hands.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do this as long as you see that the child's diaper has become soiled, then take off the diaper, clean the child, and apply Egyptian ointment to the child, and put it back on the pillow in the same way.

et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	Then I will insert or leave a needle in any uncut areas as long as it is safe, and if it is necessary to use medicinal herbs, then do so.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	And this is the form of the instrument to purge the head, as we distill the oils and medicines or needles.
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And it should be made of silver or gold, resembling a hanging lamp, like a needle, and it is led in the same way.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	And if you see, if I make a needle closed, and it is the plains that are used to purge the head.
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	and hold the head of the shoulder to keep it steady when heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	And of the char for the head.
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Many times the head of the shoulder is not a disease called "telul", and it grows and becomes large, until it is seen as something to be looked at.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	And that's why you need to cut it at the beginning, and then put the oste on fire, and then use the cauterization or burning medicine.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	And if you delay it as much as it is large, then if it is hard, of a dark color, and poor sense:
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	if you do not cut it with iron because it is an enchanted wound, because if you cut it once, there is always great pain for the patient;

And if the patient is in pain, not due to shock but from actual harm, you can see that it can be controlled if the surgeon is skilled and takes care not to cause further harm, and cure the limb of things that are loose and restrained.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	When the joint is cut and bruised
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	Said that when a solution for continuation comes from one of these cartilages, it does not last long, and is only in some people.

et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then stitch the lips together with a stitch, and treat them as soon as they are healthy.

des apostemes des levres	2. of the abscesses of the lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	In the hands of skilled surgeons, the lips of abscesses are often hard and look like grains of sand, and they can be larger or smaller;
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	Therefore, you must turn the lips of the abscesses, and cut them on each side, and take them out with tweezers and close each part;

de la char des gencives	Of the thigh bone
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	Many times, on the old cheeks, which they call "alabaster";
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	if you must hold it with your nails, and the cord at its root, and let go of the bow or the wound.

si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	If there is no return after the cauterization;

des sordens	of soreness
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	No times are assembled at the head of the teeth, the teeth are inserted between the lips, gums that are ugly and sharp.
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	And no time is the black and yellow tooth, until corruption comes to the lip, and it becomes the tooth.
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	If it comes to your notice that you must hold the patient between your hands, and the head is in your holy place, and you pull out the teeth or gums visible, as long as it does not cost anything.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	and I make of black and green, and of yellow and other stains, as much as they are needed.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	and if one has this at the first reason, it is good.
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	if not, then repeat the second part and the third, as long as you have everything.
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	and you should know that the teeth have the ability to take on various forms of wisdom teeth, according to what the one who demonstrates it does, because the raspers used to remove teeth have other shapes than those used between the teeth.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	and these forms and others should be with you prepared.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	It is necessary when you treat the patient's tooth pain that you postpone it as much as possible and as long as you can, because it should not be done quickly.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	because it is a substance high in moisture, therefore there is no excuse to delay.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	When the patient is forced to take medicine, then you must be sure of the tooth's pain.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the pain of the patient's tooth has passed, and make sure it is not damaged, and treat the root of the tooth.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	and the patient will not return to pain until the tooth is extracted, as long as it is not extracted, because we have already wanted to do this for these healthier ones.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	When you are sure that the tooth is decaying, if it comes to removing the entire tooth, scrape it thoroughly with a sharp tool to protect the gum of all parts.
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	Then the mouse has its way with you or it pricks you slightly at first and then firmly, until they are well set, then it affirms the nails.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	and let the shoulder of the patient be between your hands, and hold it firmly so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After the tooth is extracted sensibly with forceps, and if it does not slip, then take none of these strings and pull lightly on each part, and move it as you have done first.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	And if the den is perceived and mangled, then you must fill it with cloths, either the wounds are.
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	and if the extraction is made subtly with nails, so that it does not break in the extraction.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	And it is wise to over the thigh to remove the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	And be very careful not to break the tooth, and there will remain a part, and it will return to the patient due to the malice of the root and greater pain in the first.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And make sure that you do not make mistakes like those that the ignorant healers make, who through their haste and their recklessness never break a bone, and do not injure it except for what we have counted.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	but bring it about never once by the pressure of that great disease, either by the roots which they press, or by the bone which they break, as we often want.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	And when the gum is dry, wash the part with wine or vinegar and soap.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	And if they become inflamed and are lost, which often happens, use the powder of green glass.
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	If this does not work, then the patient should have the fire cautery.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The forms of the wisdom teeth, if they do not protrude at first, are long and thick, and will not double in size until you pull the tooth;
et ce sont les formes:	And these are the forms:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And they should be thick members if they do not break when ground, and they should be made of good iron, and they should be teeth that can be held tightly.
de la racine des dens	of the root of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root of the tooth is pulled, if you can put it in the socket for one or two hours, until it is smooth, then the tines called "alveoli" will be loosened, and the gums will look like they are well-groomed;
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	And these are the forms:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not come out of all these thorns, then it comes that you pull out the whole branch at the root, and put in the instrument called "athali", which is known as a "palinch", and its shape is like this:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	And so be it, and let it be large if it does not break through, and if its root jumps by this, it is well.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	If that does not happen, then help from all the stimulants and the shapes will come after:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait II rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you use it with two rains, then the shape is like this:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other instruments that are before in the reason of the teeth, and with this instrument which seems like great thorns, whose shape is like this:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	And let the stimulants be large enough that it cannot break, and may have a strong smell of stimulants:
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	and other stimulants, which are not small:
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	And the master tools are used by themselves, according to what their uses and the disease they demonstrate, because there are many diseases or the ancients did not teach different instruments for the diversity of bones and the horseshoe does not break at the end or other bones, or it pours out, if you seek as stimulants that I have said, and help with gestures, of which this is the form:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And let them be large and well-held by holding the bone, so it does not slip, but can hold and rest.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	Then restore the body to the appropriate medicines, and if there is inflammation in the bone, and it is small, then use all of this instrument.
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When the tooth appears to not fit according to the natural body, and its form is misshapen, and at the same time in women with multiple teeth, if it comes out after the tooth, and it is not in its right place, and it cannot be soaked or softened:
adonques lou raie;	then the root.
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	If it is bitten by a tooth, then use this instrument whose form is like the small tooth, and it should be made of iron, not sharp:
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And quickly and quickly in the hands, for the hardness of the teeth, and because you do not move the others, and if it appears like this, then you can tie it with a part of the rope as this is formed:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	and it is used as the claw of the fish we make for the eagles;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	and in the claw of the tooth, it is very lightly held in the hands, so that it does not move until it falls;
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	then the end is flat for any rasping, and if the teeth are too sharp and they cut the tongue, then it is necessary to smooth the file as much as possible, so that it does not cut the tongue or corrupt the speech.
quant li dent lochent	When the teeth rot
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When the tooth in front of the gum, or by percussion or by listening, and the patient cannot press on it because it hurts, and you treat them with restraining medicines, and it does not help.
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	If they are restrained with a gold thread, because the silver threads turn green and blister, but the gold does not move.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	and that the silver threads are neither too thick nor too thin, according to the space between the teeth.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	and if you see the teeth erupting, then take the thread and pull double between the two healthy teeth, then put the threads between the crooked teeth, as long as you see progress in the healthy tooth on the other side.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	Then continues the covering just where you left off, and gently and wisely draw back your hand, so it does not move at all.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	and keep your finger at the root of the tooth so it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then fit the crowns onto the pins, and assemble them, and place them between the healthy tooth and the one that is being fixed, and make sure it does not touch the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	And then leave it as wide as possible, and if it does not hold, or the pins come out, then use another pin.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	If it does not hold and serves its purpose, and is the shape of the teeth and the placement of the two healthy second molars and the two third molars, as you see:
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when the tooth is set, if it is put back in its place, as we have said.
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	and does not move a single hair that is not sharp and painful, and never takes the form of a bone of a sheep, and it is put back in its place or where it belongs, and it is tightened as we have said, and holds firmly, and remains so as we have described.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	Of the copper wire of the tongue
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	Never has a case been seen where the tongue or its flesh comes out, which is not known.
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	or by chance of wounding;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	and the operations are such that you open the mouth of the patient, and put their head in your mouth, and hold the tongue gently.
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	Then pull the nervous and large ligament as far as possible, until the tongue is free from its place, and if it does not return or out, and that is a serious wound, if it bites the uncinate and pulls wide the nearby ligament;
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	and make sure the tooth does not cut too deeply, because the artery that is there is very small;
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	and when you have finished, if the lip is red and swollen, or cold, then place the tongue in a cloth tent;
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	and the salve should be applied to the patient's lips every night, so that the wound can heal;
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	And if the dislocation occurs, then place the arm in a splint.
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	And if it does not heal, then use a slow-healing cauterization on the cauterization, which is good for this.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	Then apply another treatment as soon as it is healthy.
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	And if you see that the wound is red or black or hard, and the patient does not feel pain, if it does not hurt, because it is a gangrene.
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	And if the patient is declining into chlorosis and there is moisture, if it gushes blood, and they apply a subtle sponge, and they extract from one part and another;
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	And if you do not want to harm your patient, then use hot iron wires as soon as they are burned, and then return to your work as soon as you have finished everything.
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then lift the leg of silk and thread, and treat other treatments as soon as it is healthy.
des apostemes de la gorge	gums of the chin
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	No time comes when the gums called "godath" are called "godath," and they are properly called "hamanders." When you treat them, as we have said in the division, and they are not healthy, then keep them.
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	If it is a small, hard aphthous ulcer of dark color, and you do not touch it with any iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	And if it is red and the root is large, and not touched with iron at all, then for the evacuation of blood.
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	But let it remain until it is dead, and therefore you will leave it, or it will break by itself.
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	And if it is watery-colored and the root is fine, and you have prepared the instrument well, but first see if the abscess pus is reduced and calmed.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	Then place the patient in front of the sun, and their head should be in your hand, and they open their mouth and grip the tongue between their hands, and press the tongue against all the instruments, as you will see the form.
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	Et soit d'argent ou d'arain subtil aussi comme uns coutelz:
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	Cant tu press the tongue against all this instrument, and you see the aposteme, if take the pin and the hook in the amber, and the tail will be further than you please.
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	And try nothing with the threads, then the crown of the instrument, of which it seems some forces are.
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	And the head is all sharp, and one place to another, and are very sharp, and is made of iron or steel.
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	If you do not have this instrument present, if you have needles, then the form is like this:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	And it is cutting from one side and the other, and named.
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	When you have grasped one of the hamstrings, if you grasp the other in the same manner, and after incising it with a hot, sharp knife, and cutting along the tendon, and if blood comes out, if the tendon is seared, or gallstones are cooked, or stones from the gallbladder are removed, and similar things, as long as it is not infected.
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then the treatment continues as long as it is healthy.
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	And never do other abscesses appear in the throat than the two hamstrings, if they are cut out like the two hamstrings.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	And I treated a woman with an abscess that was not in the mouth, which is to say the abscess is of small sensation.
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	and had I closed almost all the throat, so that the woman could not breathe through the clogged duct, and could not drink or eat, and died if she lingered for one or two days.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	The abscess was so large that it required two incisions through the two holes.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	I therefore had to perform a tracheotomy, then the patient became worse, and there was a large portion of bowel exposed.
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	then another part was removed from the other side of the neck, and I opened the mouth and pressed on the tongue.
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	After filing the gallstone in these abscesses, and cutting off a part, and it does not become larger than a drop of blood.
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	and the woman's guide was torn from her mouth, and began to drink water and then wine, and did not stop trimming this abscess for a long time.
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	and the abscess dislocated further, and filled the joint I had opened, as much as it could hold, without causing great pain.
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	Therefore, I operated on it and burned the joint of the jaw:
ensi demora sens croistre;	and it did not grow further.
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	I will begin from these parts, and I alone shall do this for you, God willing.
de l’uve	Of the urethra
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	When the finger is pulled towards the nail, and it is long and thin, it is called "perpendicular".
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	And if it is too thin and round, it is called "nail".
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	When the wound is treated as we have described in the division, and the cure does not benefit, you will see that the incision is calmed and it is subtle, so you can cut it.
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	And the one that is round and assembled and is not long.
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	And if it is bloody or colored or black, you must throw away the incision of it.
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	For there is great danger for the patient.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	It is therefore necessary, as you see, according to the method I have said, of the belly and length, that you set the patient facing the sun, and press the tongue on the instrument we have made memorable before.
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	Then cut the gallbladder in the urethra, and the tail off, and the cover it with the two incisions I mentioned in the incision of the two amandras.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	And it is necessary that you do not cover more than the excess that is over the natural termination.
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	For if you cover more, you will grieve to the voice and speech.
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	After the incision, use what we have said in the incision of two thumbs, and treat it as soon as it is healed.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	And if the patient suffers from pain in the other side, then you should use an engine for the fire cautery of the other side.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	And the manner of cauterization is sharp when it is hot.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	And the patient places his head on your shoulder, and then presses the tongue with the instrument we have mentioned in the cauterization chapter of this book, and confines it with live coals, if it is not too thick or too clear;
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	and by using the thickness of this instrument, the form is:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	And if the head has a hair or puts in the medicine, like the hairs of a comb, and places the instrument on all the medicine under the eye;
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	and the patient is gasping at their cost, if the saliva and foam come from the medicine given, if it does not descend to the throat and jaw,
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	then hold your hand on all the medicine and press on the vein, the amount of the one hour's worth of medicine, as long as you see it is clear and the medicine's bitterness is soothing.
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	and if you see, take cotton and wrap it around no instrument, and moisten the cotton with the medicine, and dip the instrument in all the cotton in the case, as long as the cotton is damp at the vein.
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	And I do this often, until the cauterization is perfect, then it leaves it to dry, and I wait four or five days.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	And if you have experience in re-cauterizing medical wounds, if it is necessary to do so again, and after the cauterization, wrap the end of the urethra with rags, and clean what is outside of the medical wound.
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you have a sore throat, and use gargles as needed.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	This treatment is safer than incision, only the cauterization.
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	If it is treated with fumigation according to this method, take a lamp, and put in it incense, oak leaves, rosemary, chamomile, and any other herbs you have, and assemble them all or none of them into one pot, and let it boil;
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	And it can be well glued with strong earth, and it has an instrument made according to this manner:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	And it can be of silver or gold, and some of the ends are inserted in the mouth of the patient as much as possible until the vapor rises through the canal, until the canal is hardened;
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	After the wound has often healed, until the canal is dry and keep in mind that you should not do this at the beginning of the onset of the abscess, because many things come afterwards;
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	and only do this when the onset of the abscess has occurred;
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	And if this instrument is not present, then take a catheter and put it in the patient's mouth, if the mouth is too dry.
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	For the catheter of urine does not burn the mouth, and it is a good cure together with salvation.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	Many times it has happened in the throat of the gargle or spine of fish, or nothing at all.
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	Therefore, if you must try what you see, and press the tongue against the sun with all the instrument, so that you can see the thing.
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	And if it does not open you, then you must make the patient vomit, unless the meat is cooked in the stomach.
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	If by chance the thing is accomplished through vomiting;
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	or the patient swallows a sponge piece, or a navel piece, or a lactice root, or a piece of dry bread;
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	and holds the sponge by the end and then glues it;
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	and when it reaches the shoulder, if it will, and then draws forth a string;
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	and if it does not come from what we have said, then use the instrument of plucking according to this form:
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	And let the hooks be placed at the head if it can more gently enter into the mouth, and have the head raised above;
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	And you must not touch the epigastrium, for all will avoid it, and do not force the bones.
