Et li restoracion si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, et li met I cussin entre les espaules, puis presse les espaules, et li assemble les costes des II costelz a tes mains, et subtilie dou mettre igal a toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que li figure de l’os soit si com il covient;	And the restoration is when the patient feels pain on their chest, and the spine is set between the shoulders, then press the shoulders, and assemble the ribs of the two costels at your hands, and subtly put them all in the way that you can, as long as the bone feels like it should;
puis met sus emplaustres et estoupes desus l’estele subtil de salz, ou d’autre fust legier, et l’envoloupe en I drapeil, et la lie sus l’os brisiet, si qu’elle ne se mueve;	Then apply splints and bandages over the subtle surface of salt or another light substance, and wrap it around the broken bone, so that it does not move.
et torne le liien reondement au dos, et l’estraint avenanment, et rewarde chescune houre la liure, et s’elle ramolist, si l’estraint;	And turn the tie around the back, and hold it tightly, and reward each hour with a drink, and if it loosens, then tighten it.
et s’il lou covient desliier, por corrosion ou por prurite que vient au leu, ou dolor ou aposteme, si te haste, et lou deslie, et raie l’emplaustre, et adresce ceu qui i est venus de manieres de cures;	And if it comes loose due to corrosion or pruritus of the limb, or pain or gangrene, and loosens, and loosens the bandage, and adjust the splint, and address what came from the ways of treatments.
puis ramoinne l’emplaustre, et l’estraint tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then reset the guide, and hold it as long as it is stable.
de la brisure des costes	Of the fracture of the ribs
Saiches que li briseure des costes ne vient fuer que en leus gros aprés le dos, et au chief dedens, et ne ploient fuer que por ceu qu’eles sont glairouses;	Fractures of the ribs only occur after the back is broken, and at the top of the chest, and they do not break for any other reason, as they are fatty.
et le sent om bien a l’inquisition as dois.	And it feels well in the examination as it should.
Et li restoremens si est que tu met igal la brisure, si com il covient.	And the restoration is if you put the fracture in place as it should be.
Et puis met l’emplaustre, et l’estraint d’une estele, se tu en as mestier.	Then place the plaster and draw it tightly with a steel bandage, if you have the skill for it.
Et se li brisure des costes est declinans au dedens, si sent li malaides tres grant dolor, et pointure, ausi com de pleuresin, car li os point la toile;	And if the rib fracture is inclined towards the chest, it feels very painful and pointed, like labor pains, because the bone does not cover the skin.
et alaine a poinnes, et toust et vomist grant planteit de sanc, et c’est de grief santeit, et li ancien i ont mis grant engien.	And it has points, and all other symptoms are vomiting great quantities of blood, and this is a serious illness, and the ancients have put great emphasis on it.
Et si a de ces qui dient qu’il le covient aministrer viandes qui enflent le ventre, por bouter la briseure au defuer.	If it is said that it should be administered meat that inflames the belly, by fastening the girdle around the loins.
Nos ne faisons mie ceu, que apostemes chaulz n’i viegne, s’il n’i est venus.	We do not do this, as it is not necessary to have apostemes if it has not come.
Et s’il i est venus, si le saine.	And if it has come, then it is the right one.
Et dirent aucun d’ous c’on met ventouses sor le leu, por sucier forment, et c’est semblant a raison;	And say no one puts forceps on the leg, for they form like reason.
toutevoie, doutance i a que li ventouse n’atraie les superfluitez au leu por la disposition de foiblece.	However, it is not certain that the forceps do not cause doubt when the leg has too much tissue due to its position.
Et dirent aucun d’ous c’on doit covrir le leu de lainne moillie en oile chaut, et met on tentes entre les costes por metre igal la lieure entor, puis soit curez de la cure de pleurisin, de viande et de medicine.	And none of them say that they should cover the throat with oiled wool and put tents between the ribs to measure the length of the rib cage, then treat the pleurisy, meat, and medicine.
Et se li malaides sent grant dolor qu’il ne puet soffrir par l’os qui point la toile, et doutance est au malaide, si covient fendre sus lou leu de la coste brisie, et covient mettre desoz I estrument por warder lou syfac;	And if the patient feels great pain that they cannot endure due to the bone not piercing the tissue, and doubt is in the patient, then it is necessary to cut off the shoulder of the coste brisie and put an instrument to hold the face.
et adonques doit on trenchier l’os, et traire legierement, et puis coudre les II levres de la plaie, s’elle est grans, et le curez d’emplaustres, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And therefore, one must break the bone, draw it lightly, and then cut the lips of the wound if they are large, and treat them with plasters as soon as possible.
Et se apostemes chaus vient, si met sus drapelz moilliez en oile roset, et met sus lou leu;	If the abscess pops, then put on the cloth that is greasy with oil of rose, and put it on the leg.
et cure tandis le leu de ceu qu’il covient a aposteme, et soit gisans sovins sus lou costeit ou il doit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat the leg while it is dislocating, and put on the cloth that is greasy with oil of rose, as long as it is healthy.
de la brisure dou col	Of the break of the shoulder
Aucune fois vient briseure as os dou col, et poc avient k’il ploie;	No breakage ever comes to the bone of the knee, and it never happens when it slips.
et ausi a l’espinee dou dos.	And also to the spine of the back.
Et quant ce avient a aucun, et tu vues savoir s’il sera sanez ou non, si pren warde se tu vois ses mains mollifiies et enflees et mortes, et ne les puet movoir ne estendre, et quant tu les poins d’une aguille, si ne lou sent.	When nothing comes to help, and you see if it will be healthy or not, if you see your hands soft and swollen and lifeless, and cannot move or stretch them, and when you prick them with a needle, if they do not feel.
Saiches qu’il est mortelz em plusors dispositions, et s’il les muet et sent bien quant on les estraint et point, saiches que li jointure de l’os est sauve, et que li malaides iert curez, s’on i met cure.	Dangerous are those who die in many ways, and if they are silent and feel well when extracted and not stretched, dangerous ones that the joint of the bone is saved, and that the patient will be cured, if we put them under care.
Et se semblans chose vient a l’espinee dou dos, et tu vues savoir s’il iert sanez ou non, si pren warde se li piez sont amollis, et se li accident i sont qui sont em mains, et sus lou dos saut ventositeit et egestion sens volonteit;	And if something similar comes to the spine of the back, and you see whether it is healthy or not, if you take care of the bones that are soft, and the accidents that are in the hands, and on the back there is a jump and vomiting with will;
et quant on l’a sovineit sus son ventre, si saut egestion sens volonteit.	When it is removed from its place under the belly, it seems to come out willingly.
Et quant il est sovinez sus son dos et il vuet asseller, si ne puet.	And when he feels pain on his back and sees it swelling, if he can.
Saiches qu’il est mortelz:	Severe cases that are fatal:
si ne laboreir mie en sa cure.	If they do not labor much in their care.
Et se cist accident ne li vienent, si est li chose plus legiere.	And if this accident does not come, it is the lighter thing.
Et li cure si est que tu rewardes s’il i a aposteme chaut, si met sus l’espinee oile roset ou oile de moieuf d’uef, tant qu’il soit apaisiez;	And the treatment is to reward it if it has an abscess, by putting on oil rose or oil of mustard seed until it is calmed.
puis met sus un des emplaustres confortans et sechans, et le lie d’un liien, et comande au malaide a reposer;	Then put on a comforting plaster and let it dry, and tie it with a cord, and command the patient to rest.
et ne dorme mie sus celle partie ou il sent la dolor, tant k’il soit sanez.	And do not sleep on that part where the pain is felt, as long as it is healthy.
Et se aucuns os se dessevre, si covient coper sus lou keur;	If any bones break, then cover them with a cloth.
et oste l’os, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie, s’elle est grans, a une costure, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if the bone is large, assemble the two sides of the wound with a stitch as much as possible, then apply a poultice made of uncooked wool, until it is healthy.
et se li chiés de l’os est brisiez, ki est apelez li «chiés de la kowe», se i boute ton pouchet de ta main senestre, et le met igal a l’autre main a ton pooir, puis met l’emplaustre et l’estele sus, se tu en a mestier;	If the head of the bone is broken, which is called the "head of the bone", take your left hand packet and place it in the other hand on the part where it hurts, then put the splint and the bandage over it, if you can.
puis l’estraint, et s’il i a os desevreit, si fent sus, et l’oste, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee.	Then hold it steady, and if it has broken bones, then cut them off, and the bone, and dress the wound as much as possible when it is healthy.
de la brisure de l’os de la hainche	Of the fracture of the hip bone
Poc avient que li os de la hainche soit brisiez, et s’il avient, si n’avient fuer c’un poc d’amenuisement au chief;	A sudden injury occurs when the shinbone is broken, and if it does, it is not usually a serious matter at the ankle.
et fent dou lonc, et decline au pardedens, et vient au malaide dolor au leu, et pointure, et enfle ceu que brise.	The broken bone becomes long and twisted, causing pain in the jaw, teeth, and surrounding tissues, and the broken piece is felt.
Et li restoration si est que tu estendes ta main sus, tant que tu soies sus la briseure;	If you extend your hand over the broken bone as far as the fracture site, the repair can be made.
et saiches quelz est li brisure et li figure de li;	Inspect the break and its position to determine the best course of treatment.
et se li brisure est au chief soulement, si met igal cele brisure, tant qu’ele soit a figure natureil.	If the break is only at the ankle, place the fracture in proper alignment and hold it there until it heals naturally.
Et se li brisure est dou lonc, ou elle decline au dedens, si fai gesir le malaide sus son ventre, tant que li restauration de cele brisure te soit aparillie.	And if the fracture is long or it declines into the dens, then I command the patient to lie on his stomach as much as possible, until the restoration of this fracture is clear.
Et quant tu l’avras mise igal, si met sus l’emplaustre, puis met sus une estele de fust ou de keur, et estraint la briseure, si qu’ele ne se mueve;	And when you have placed it evenly, then place the template on it, then place a piece of flax or thread, and tighten the knot, if it does not move.
et emple le leu desoz les costes, tant que li lieure soit igalz.	and use the shoulder blade as much as the line is even.
Et comande au malaide k’il dorme sus son costeit sain, ou sus son dos.	And command the patient to sleep on his healthy side or on his back.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si n’i tochier, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et met sus ceu que nos avons devant dit;	And if abscesses appear, and they come, if they do not hurt, then as long as the abscess does not hurt, and put what we have said before.
et puis revien a la restauration, et l’estraint si com il covient, s’il n’i a nul mavais accident;	and then return to the restoration, and tighten as much as it is possible, if there are no other accidents.
et c’est li maniere.	And that is the way.
de la brisure de l’ajutoire	Of the dislocation of the shoulder
Li adjutoires est ceu qui est entre lou coute et lou chief de l’espaule, et s’il est brisiez, si le doit on restorer selonc l’une des II manieres:	The helper is that which is between the rib and the shoulder blade, and if it is broken, then it should be restored according to one of the following ways:
dont l’une est que tu pren I fust plain de moiene groissor, selonc ceste forme:	One way is to use a piece of flat stone, according to this form:
Et lie as II chiés II liens, et les pent en haut, et siece li malaide sus I siege;	And place the heads of the bones in this way, and hold them up, and put the patient on his side.
puis li giete som bras brisiet sus le fust, tant qu’il viegne a l’aissele, et ait em mi une corbeure de fust, puis pent sus aucune pesant chose ou li ministres l’estende aval;	Then the patient's broken arm is placed on the flat stone, until it reaches the shoulder, and has a small hole in the stone, then it can be used for no heavy thing or to extend the hand.
puis mette li mires la briseure igal a ses mains ensamble, tant que li briseure retorne si com il covient.	Then put the forceps evenly in your hands, as long as the forceps return to its original position.
Et li autre maniere si est que on sovine le malaide sus son hatereil, et li lie la main a son col, puis comande a II ministres que li uns teigne ceu qui est sus la briseure a ses mains, et li autres teigne desoz a tout I liien, et estende chescuns a sa partie.	And the other way, if one cuts the patient's hair too short, and grasps their hand at the wrist, then commands the ministers to touch the parts that are bare on the patient's hands, and then touch the rest of the limb without touching anything else, and extend each part to its place.
Et se tu vues que li estraction soit plus fors, si estraint I liien desoz la briseure, et sus la briseure, et estende chescuns des ministres a sa part.	And if you see that the extraction is too painful, then force the limb away from the bracelet, and remove the bracelet, and extend each of the ministers to its place.
Et se li briseure est prochiene au chief de l’espaule, si covient que tu mettes I liien moien desoz l’assele, et I autre vers lou coute, desoz la briseure;	And if the forceps is near the shoulder blade, then you should put one ligament on the other side of the shoulder, and the other on the other side.
et ausi se li briseure est devers lou coute, si i covient mettre I liien legierement, sens labor, tant que li briseure soit igalz sus lou leu, et sus lou coute;	And if the forceps is towards the elbow, then you should lightly put the ligaments on either side of the shoulder, as long as the forceps is even with the shoulder and the elbow.
puis met igal la brisure, si com il covient, et l’estraint, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	Then place the forceps evenly, as long as it is possible, and hold it steady, so that it does not move.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si ne l’estraindre mie jusc’a VII jors, et met sus lainne moillie en aisil et en oile roset, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez;	When the abscess pus comes out, if it is not strained for seven days, and it is rubbed with fine oil and rosewater until the abscess pus is eased.
puis l’estraint, et li maniere de l’estraindre si est que tu mettes l’emplaustre sus la briseure, puis assemble le bras sus l’ajutoire, et met ta main sus l’espaule ou sus lou sein;	Then strain it, and the way to strain it if you place the plaster on the wound, then gather the arm with the helper, and place your hand on the shoulder or on the chest.
et met le drapeil, et estraint sus l’ajutoire, et sus lou bras, si que li bras soit en leu d’esteles, s’aucune chose ne le te deffent, ou se li os n’est muez.	And tie the bandage, and strain it with the helper and on the arm, if the arm is in the elbow, nothing will stop you, or if the shoulder is not moved.
Et se tu doutes que li os ne se mueve, si use d’esteles, et met sus la brisure une estele plus large et plus fort des autres, et ait entre chescune estele I doi d’espaice, et soit chescune estele si grans qu’elle passe la briseure III dois de chescune part;	If you doubt that the bone does not move, use these, and place the cutting on a larger and stronger bone than the others, and have between each cut one space of two spaces, and make each space as large as it passes the break three times of each part.
puis estrain sus les esteles, ensi com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre sus la briseure, plus fort et moins en aloignant.	Then draw the saws, as I said at the beginning of this chapter, making them stronger and less slanted.
Et se tu vois l’assise des esteles, et l’estrignement, si com nos avons dit, en l’oure que tu restoures le membre brisiet, et tu doutes l’aposteme chaut, si le laisse a liier jusc’a septime jor, si com nos avons dit;	If you see the seat of the saws and the stretching, as we have said, in the bone that you are resetting the broken member, and you doubt the grip, if it leaves it to tighten in the ninth day, as we have said.
puis regarde chescuns III jors lou lien, que prurite ne enfleure n’i viegne au leu, ou li norrissemens ne puist venir au membre por ceu k’il est trop estrois.	Then look at each of the three years, whether the link is itchy or does not come to the skin, or the incisions do not come to the limb because it is too tight.
Si l’adrece, si com nos avons dit.	If the address, as we have said.
Et se nulz telz accidens n’i vient, si ne lou desliier fuer que aprés III jors ou plus, et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ait ses mains sus son stomac;	And if there are no such accidents, then it should be done, unless after three years or more, the patient falls asleep and has his hands on his stomach.
et met desoz l’ajutoire I cussin plain de laine igalment, et regarde chescune houre dou jor ou de la nut, que li figure dou membre brisiet ne se mueve, ou ne soit amollis li liiens;	And then place the assistant in a plain linen bandage, and look at each hour of the day or night, whether the broken limb does not move, or is not smoothed by the ligatures.
si l’adrece par la vertu de medicine, et li done la viande que nos avons devant mis, en teil maniere que li viande soit au premier subtilz;	If the address is by the virtue of medicine, and it is the meat that we have before us, in part as to make the meat subtle at first.
et quant il comance a reprendre, si soit grosse.	And when it comes time to take it back, if it is large.
Et est costume que li ajutoire et li jambe doient estre repris en XL jors dou tout;	And it is customary that the helper and the leg should be taken back in XL jors of everything.
et adonques lou doit on desliier et aministrer bain et medicines d’oignemens por le leu adrecier.	And therefore, it must be deshed and administered with baths and remedies for the wound to be healed.
Et se li estricture est laide et emboee, si demore a desliier L jors ou II mois.	And if the stricture is thick and blocked, it should be desisted for 4 to 6 weeks.
de la brisure du bras	of the shoulder fracture
Li bras est compos de II os, qui sont apelez li dui «foscile», de coi li uns est petis, et est cil qui enseut le pouchet;	The arm is composed of two bones, which are called the "femur" and "tibia", and one of them is smaller, and it is this one that forms the pouch.
et li autres est grans, et est cil qui est desoz, devers lou petit doi;	and the other is large, and it is the one that is distorted, towards the small doe.
par aventure brise li grans foscile soulement, ou li petis, et par aventure andui ensamble.	by chance, only the large fleshy part, or the small one, and by chance, together with the eyes.
Quant li petis fosciles est brisiez, li restaurations est legiere, et li sanations;	When the small fleshy parts are broken, the restoration is lighter, and the cures.
et quant li grans est brisiez, si est li sanation male, et plus griés que quant il sont brisiez andui ensamble.	and when the large ones are broken, if it is a poor cure, and more painful than when they are broken together.
Se c’est li petis foscile qui est brisiez soulement, si le covient poc estendre legierement, et mettre igal.	If only the small splints are broken, it is best to extend them lightly and make them even.
Et se c’est li grans foscile, si le covient estraindre plus fort;	And if it is the large fleshy part, then it must be stretched more forcefully.
et l’estende sus I cussin, et teigne le pouchet de la main plus haut des autres, et li petis dois plus bas des autres dois, et soit li malaides croisiez sus lui meisme, et I cussin devant lui plus haut, que li malaides ne soffre nule labor;	and extend it over the thumb, and stretch the palm of the hand higher than the others, and the small ones must be lower than the others, and the patient should be crooked over it, and the thumb in front of it, so that the patient does not suffer any labor.
puis estende li ministres som bras a la partie desoz a sa main, ou a I liien, et uns autres ministres a I autre au desus.	Then extend the muscles of the arm to the part opposite the hand, or to the elbow, and some other muscles to the other end.
Et puis le mette li mires igal, selonc sa millor forme.	And then he places the head in its place, according to its best form.
Et se en la brisure a pieces, si met chescune en son leu, et s’il en i a nule desevree ke poigne lou keur, et tu ne la pues restorer en son leu, si fent sus et l’oste, si com nos avons dit devant.	And if it breaks into pieces, he places each in its place, and if there are no loose pieces that point to the bone, and you cannot restore it to its place, then as we have said before, set the bone and the head.
Et se avec la briseure a plaie, je en ai parleit au chapistre singuler;	And if with the force of the wound, I have spoken to the single surgeon;
si pren la cure.	if it is treated.
Et se en l’encomencement dou restorement sorvient apostemes chaus, si glue I drapeil de cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire blainche, que ne soit mie ne trop durs ne trop molz;	And if in the beginning of the restoration, abscesses occur that are difficult to remove, if the dressing made of olive oil and wax is not too soft or too hard, it should be.
et lie I drapeil par sus subtilment, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez.	and gently lift the dressing as long as the abscesses are soothed.
Et puis oste lou cerote, et i met l’emplaustre de la poudre dou molin avec abun d’uef, pues met les esteles, et soit li estele de la briseure adés plus fors, et un poc plus large que les autres;	And then the bone, and he puts the plaster with a lot of powder from the mill with urine, because it puts the stitches, and it is the plaster of the fracture that is further apart, and a little wider than the others.
et saiches que il doit avoir VI esteles ou bras em plusors dispositions:	and you should say that it must have six stitches or bands in more positions:
soit que li briseure soit en l’un des os, soit en II;	that the fracture is in one of the bones, or in two:
et estraint plus sus la briseure que autre part, et toz jors moins en aloignant, si com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre;	and is pulled more under the fracture than elsewhere, and less by moving away, as I said at the beginning of this chapter:
et soient li drapelz que sont sus la briseure molz et moistes, et ne soient mie dur ne aspres;	and be the bandages that are under the wet and moist fracture, and not be too hard or rough:
et soit li filz, dont il est estrains, de lin, ne trop gros ne trop menus, si com nos avons dit.	And let it be the son, who is far away, from the lion, not too large nor too small, as we have said.
Et rewarde lou membre et lou liien aprés aucuns jors.	And reward the member and the limb after some years.
Et se aucuns mavais accidens vient au membre, si com prurite ki vient au membre, si covient que tu aroses lou membre d’aigue chaude, tant que cil prurites soit apaisiez;	And if any harm comes to the member, if it is like pruritus to the member, then you must wash the member with hot water as long as the pruritus is calmed.
et laisse le membre ne mie estroit reposer.	and let the member rest without being too tight.
Et puis rencomence l’estrignement, et se li liiens est amolis et li os desevrez, et semblant chose, si l’adresce.	And then the inflammation resumes, and if the limb is smoothed and the bones are revealed, and it seems like something, if it is removed.
Et se pren warde se li norrissemens ne puet venir au membre, por ceu qu’il est trop estrois, si covient que tu l’amollisses I poc, et laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant que li norrissemens i corre, et puis l’estraint.	And if the swelling is not coming to the member because it is too swollen, because there are no poultices that can relieve it, and let it rest for some time until the swelling decreases and then extract it.
Et se nules de ces choses que nos avons dit ne vient au malaide, si ne lou desliier jusc’a XX jors.	If these things do not come to the patient, if he does not loosen the dressing for 20 years.
ou enqui entor, puis li pent les mains a son col, et soit ses cols igalz, et se warde de movement et de degitement, et dorme sus son dos;	Or if it is necessary to examine the chest, then one can put their hands on the chest, and the chest should be even, and it should be quiet and calm, and it should sleep on its back.
et saiches que ceste briseure est restoree en XXX jors ou en XXXV, et par aventure en XX jors, selonc les compositions et les complexions des vertus.	And you advise that this cauterization is restored in 30 days or 35 days, and by chance in 20 days, according to the compositions and complexions of the virtues.
de la brisure de la main	of the wrist fracture
Saiches que au dos de la main et as nous des dois avient poc de briseures, et n’i vient mais que ploieure maintes fois.	Wishes that on the back of the hand and in the two wrists there are few fractures, and only painful swelling many times.
Et quant li plante de la main est brisie ou ploie, si covient que li malaides siece croisiet, et siet droitement devant lui igalement;	And when the plant of the hand is broken or crushed, if it comes that the patient lies down correctly, and lies straight in front of him evenly.
puis met sa main sus la toie estendue, et estende li ministres les os brisiez, et les mete igalz li mires, tant qu’il soient bien joint;	Then the patient places their hand on the extended plank, and extends the muscles of the broken bones, and places them evenly in the joints, as long as they are well connected.
et met l’emplastre et les estoupes, se apostemes n’i vient, puis i met une estele selonc la quantiteit dou leu;	And then the patient applies plaster and bandages, and if it does not come, then they put a stopper according to the size of the limb.
et soit envoloupee en I drapeil de lin.	and is wrapped in one layer of linen.
Et se li briseure est au pardedens entor lou ventre de la plante, si fai une spere de drapelz, et comande au malaide qu’il l’estrigne a sa plante brisie;	And if the fracture is at the side of the hand, I make a ring of bandages, and instruct the patient to tighten it on their broken hand.
et puis l’estrain d’un lonc drapeil, et soit li estele de keur souef ausi grans com li plante de la main, et l’estraint, si com il covient.	Then the strain of a long, loose hair, and it is the same as the pain of being touched to the palm as large as the plant of the hand, and it is held steady, if it can be done.
Et se li brisure est au defuer, si covient que tu mettes une estele sus, et une autre desoz en la plante, si que li mains soit overte et droite, puis le lie tot entor la main, et estanche lou liien entre les dois.	If the fracture is at the neck, then if you place a splint on it and another one in the plant, if the hand is over and straight, then the bone totally enters the hand, and it is held between the two.
Et se li briseure vient a aucun des nous des dois, se c’est li pouchés, si le met igal, si com il covient;	And if the cutting comes to none of us of the two, if it is closed, then it is closed, if it can be done.
et l’estraint avec la plante, et se tu vues si met une estele droite petite por lever la briseure, et ne se mueve;	and it is held with the palm, and if you see if a straight small finger is raised to lift the cutting, and does not move.
et se li brisure est as autres dois, si com en l’indice ou l’un des autres, si le met igal, et lou lie avec lou doi sain qui est aprés;	And if the cutting is in other two fingers, if it is closed in the index or one of the others, if it is closed, and it is held with the healthy thumb that is after.
ou tu les lie toz en I tenant, que mues vaut, ou tu met sus une estele, si com ou pouchet;	If you tie them all in one knot, as much as it is worth, or if you put them on a stool, as we have experienced.
et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	and take care in the restoration and positioning of the abscess, and cut away what comes, as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	Of the broken limb
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	The head of the shoulder is often broken many times, and it can be seen when it turns forward and backward.
et li restauration si est c’on lie I liien desus la briseure, et I autre desoz.	and the restoration if it is tied with the ligaments of the fracture, and the other is loose.
Et li malaides gise sus sa faice, puis estende chescuns ministres son lien a sa part igalment;	And the patient is guided by his face, then extends each of the muscles of his limb equally.
et c’est quant li brisure est emmi l’os.	When the fracture is out of the bone.
Et se li brisure est prochiene a la racine de la cuixe, si soit li uns des liiens devers lou poignil, et li autres liiens desoz la briseure.	And if the fracture is close to the root of the limb, then some of the bones are turned away from the point of impact, and the others are broken at the fracture.
Et ausi s’elle est prochiene au genoil, et adonques soit li liens delez lou genoil, et soit li extension aval;	And if it is near the knee, then loosen the kneelinks and extend the leg.
puis mette li mires l’os igal a ses II mains, tant qu’il soit selonc sa figure natureil, et puis met l’emplaustre, et lou lie, se apostemes chaz n’i vient.	Then place the bone in its natural position and adjust it with your hands until it fits, then insert the splint and wrap it around, and do not move unless it does not fit.
Et s’il i a aposteme chaut, si le laisse apaisier puis revien a ton ovraige et a ta cure;	And if it has swelled, then leave it to rest and return to your work and treatment.
li lieure est faite en teil maniere.	The bandage is made in parts.
Il covient que tu envoloupes sus la briseure I bendeil dur doublé en II ou III, et en demoure li superfluitez, puis torne la jambe tant que li talons veigne a la racine de la naige, et boute I fil lonc entre la cuixe et la jambe, delez lou genoil desoz, et veignent li chief dou fil au desus;	It is necessary that you wrap it around the fracture, doubling it in two or three, and removing any excess, then bend the leg until the heel touches the root of the nail, and tie one end of the cord between the knees and the leg, loosening the knee joint, and let the other end of the cord go to the ankle;
puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	Then turn the leg and the thigh of the knee, then put the splint on, and put a splint on the bone of the leg.
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	Then use the seventh between the leg and the thigh of the drapery to evenly stretch the strapping, then begin to tie the third or fourth formation above the splint.
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	And as more is added to the splint, the less it is tightened.
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	Then take the two filaments that you have tied between the leg and the thigh, and tie three splints that are above them, then return to the opposite end of the knot at the chief of the filament, as long as you see the knot loose.
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	When the limb is forced to move, if it does not move from its joint, then it is left alone, and it does not come out of its abscess or swell in any other way.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	And if it happens, if it is not treated, and addresses the matter as we have said many times.
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	And if it has pieces of bone that prick, then it can be treated; it may not be possible.
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	And if it cannot be done, then the limb must be cut and drained.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	And the treatment should be done as we have said, regardless of how healthy it is.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	And no time is the joint broken when I place these, as in the helper arm and shoulder.
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	In the restoration made thus far, it does not creak the patient's joints.
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en L jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	And you should know that the cheekbone is restored in L years, or less than that, or more, according to the diversity of complexions.
de la ruelle dou genoil	Of the right knee joint
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	It is said that in the right knee joint there is little breaking, but it often swells.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	And if it breaks, if it is not much more than a fracture, or a puncture, and comes to all the wounds, and feels pain, and that feels okay.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	And the restoration is that it is placed even those that are loosened at both ends, as long as they can be assembled.
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	Then the template is placed, and a ring is inserted if you have the skill, and it is tightened as it should be, then reward all the adjustments we have made in other dislocations, such as clicking and other appearances.
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If there is an accident that it can happen, as long as it is healthy.
de la brisure de la jambe	Of the break of the leg
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	If the leg has two bones, then some are called "true" and others are called "false.
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	And it comes all the same as a broken arm, and for this is the restoration like that of the arm properly, and all the parts are. And if the two bones are broken together, then turn the leg from all sides.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if the small bones are broken, then turn forward.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	And if the large bones are broken, and it feels great pain, and it is seen that it is very bad.
et torne desoz.	and turn quickly.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	Then, apply extension, and place it evenly, and bend the elbow evenly.
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	However, if the fracture is ugly, and there are more pieces, then the extension should be smaller and lighter.
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	and lift it according to your strength.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	And when you have completed your task, if you take two strips of fine hair that curl on one side and the other, and are long enough to reach from the thigh to the knee.
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	Then wrap the other around the thigh and knee, and tie it tightly, and at this time do not allow the leg to lean to the right or left, and it is well.
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	And no one has ever maintained a long leg without pain, and it has been found to be true, and they put it on the leg to warn of movement, and it is truly made in the fracture or wound.
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	And shakes every leg to see if it has an abscess or no other accident.
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the treatment is as long as it is healthy.
de la brisure des os dou piet	Of the break of the bones so large
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	At the ankle there is no breaking of bones, but the large bones break never, and you must be careful not to break them in more positions.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	And if there comes as much pain in the fracture as it is, and you see these bones over each other, then put them so that the top one is on the ground, just as it was when it was flying, and then now put your foot on the knee that was injured, and lift the bones as much as they seem to be in their places;
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	Then place the cauterization instrument and extinguish it, and make a small incision in the lower part of the belly, then draw out the pus through the hole, then wrap the wound with lint and other things that you have skill in.
Et quant III jors ou IIII seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	When three or four days have passed, if the bone is not healed, you will find the bones unevenly broken, dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	And if there are any of the two fractures, if they are restored, then as we have said, use your hand.
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	Then place on the other fracture a splint according to its length, and make a larger incision, then draw out that same hole you mentioned, and draw out the pus through the hole.
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	And if there are more than two fractures, or more, if you make a splint for each one according to its quantity, wrapped in one layer of lint and draw out the hole through the hole.
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	And let it be situated under the head of the tableau, if the belly is not too full, in order to draw it well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	And you must not ignore other things that I have said at other times, as soon as we have said them.
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	and cut out every accident as it comes.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	of the fracture of the bone of the point
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	When the bone of the woman's nature is broken, if it is set in place, then it leans towards the side of the full belly, and it should be held by the ribs.
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	Then fill the bone with the natural material of the patient's cloth, and put it in as thick as I do.
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	Then the woman is turned, and her back is gently bent a little at a time, and then she jumps on the cotton, as soon as it comes into contact with nature, and returns the bone with the stone.
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	And when she sees blood, if the cotton is wet, and when she has bled, it is reset, and in seven days or less, it is healed.
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	If the fracture is restored, and if you see, take a bowl of bloodroot, and tie it around the wound, and pour all the blood into nature.
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	Then blow into the cinnamon while the bowl is being emptied.
la nature si revenra li brisure;	The nature so returns to the fracture;
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then it is filled with cotton, and it leaves no scars, as long as it is healthy.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	And when the bone of the elbow is broken, or of the woman, if it is repaired as we have said in the bone of the shoulder;
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	and these fractures are not hidden from those who study and use it, and they read my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	For the fracture indicates in more positions the right way of the restoration:
enten le donques.	read the following.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	In the garden, when it is broken, take an goose's grip and bite the garden;
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	1. Then wrap the wound with drapes, and leave it for three days, and it will heal quickly.
de brisure avec plaie	Of a fracture with wound
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for the one who has a fracture with wound, even if it is large, as the bone of the shoulder or elbow or appearance, that he be healthy now, if the wounds that we have said testify to it.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the healthy wound is, if the vitrol is not coming out, then continue to restore the fracture at the same hour, or the next day, if you are not able to come.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	And if you are not able to come the next day, leave the restoration until the next day, as long as you are calm and do not touch it again on the third or fourth day, because you will cause bad luck.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	If the bone is broken, it is separated at the point discovered, and if you want to put it back in place gently with your hands, at a small extension.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	2. And if the extension does not fit to put on your hands, and you have this instrument made of iron, which is seven or eight inches long, and the size is according to the quantity of the wound.
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	3. And for this reason it is necessary to pull three or four times, according to how much he has experience in each treatment of fracture.
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	4. And it should be tight and large, so it does not slip under the compression of your limb in your patient's chest, and on the other hand, it should be large in front, and wide in front, like this:
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	And is called "palinché", because it is necessary that the head of the bone be placed on the shoulder of the shaft.
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	And the bow should once again be placed, as it rises, and should be equal on both sides.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	And if the fracture is not obvious, and the strings cannot well grasp the bone, then it comes that you cover the top of the bone with the string as much as it has power.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	And if you do not bring the bone back as we have said, if it does not hold with an appropriate instrument, whether it is a chisel, an incisor, or a more suitable one, to your hand;
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	then use the one that you have found to be appropriate in the hard and small holes in the bone.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	When the bone is reset, and the patient feels great pain afterwards, it indicates that there is something wrong with its natural state.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	If you keep it in its place until it is in the shoulder, then wrap it with black vinaigre, and properly so it is;
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	and do not put anything on the wound or other parts unless it is oily, so as not to cause inflammation and decay.
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	then administer ointments as you restore the bone, and leave the wound exposed, and cover it completely, according to the size of the wound, and make sure the wound is not strained with the fracture.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	and many times have I seen this cause the man to die, and have made the patient come out of the poultice or mortify or corrode never.
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	and let the scabs be softer and more moist than those of other fractures.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	And if the wound is severe or large, and you doubt that you have had an accident, as we have said, and you feel pain in the limb, if you cannot find anyone to help;
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	but wrap it with cloth, in the limb of the wound, harden the ends, and tie them.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	When you see after the first or second day that the wound is healing, and if all that you have placed on it is beneficial for healing wounds, and if the ointment is effective and similar to what you have used.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre II fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	It is necessary that you stretch the limb twice a day, in the morning and evening, as long as it is painful and healthy.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	It is necessary that the limbs are straightened in a way that the bow can be easily moved.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	If they persist, and the bow cannot be held back, but moves forward, it is necessary that you try to hold the wound with a tent, and all these pieces that cause the pain should be realigned.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	If an abscess comes to the limb, or in any other way of corruption, if you must cure it, according to what is said in this chapter before.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	And when the bone is broken, and open the limb, as we have experienced with the bone of the arm or the helper's leg, and other similar bones of the large limbs, if you do not treat it, because many times there is death, but leave it until it bleeds;
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	by chance, the bone may heal after 20 or 30 days, then treat the wound, if you can.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	If you do not, then leave it alone.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	The first sentence to translate is: "des brus qui viennent sour la souffrance
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	We often come after the health of the fracture, but when it is near the joint, and it is a shame to see how the member looks;
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	and by chance cannot make the member its natural position.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	But if it is near us, then we must help it.
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	If the patient is given medicinal steam baths, such as aloes, incense, and myrrh, and sarcocolle, and other similar things, if you do not take any of these things, or all together, and mix them with stebold wine or with a large amount of beer or with honey;
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	and place it on the wound, and stretch it well, and do not let it slip from your hands.
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	and then let it go, and repeat another one, until the nodes are straight.
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	or you stretch a well-made piece of plaster;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	because the property of the plaster is that it holds all the flesh together;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	and if the node is already converted into hardness as well as a piercing, and it is painful to the healer, then the coping is done, and the excess is removed.
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	or you dress it with no rasping, as long as it is straight, and the cure as soon as it is healthy.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	A weak limb that is after the cast
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the bone fracture is healed, and the weak and subtle parts are recovered, if there come from the cause:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	if the other is because it was too tightly bound, and it was not well tied as it should have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	or if it has too many ties, and the nails cannot come to the member;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	or for multiplicity of bending;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	or if it has too large movements, and it is not in its place at the hour;
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	or if it lacks blood in its heart, if it is weak;
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And the treatment if you make the patient lie down, and make the heart tense, as long as it does not multiply in him;
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	And he is given water, and then he feels better and recovers.
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	Then salt is applied to the member, if it draws out the great inflammation, and often the sweat turns green, as long as the inflammation reaches the member.
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	And it returns to its natural form.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	A dislocated limb after the healing process.
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the members are twisted after restoration, and the bones are broken open, and the shape of the member is deformed, it does not follow its natural course:
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	If one does not believe the fools who say that one must break the member entirely at once, and many have done so in our land:
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	The first sentence to translate is: "et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en venti grans malz, et par aventure li mors;
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	1. All voyages, if the nodes and tortures are fresh, if they can be raised with hot water, or if the mollifying herbs are cooked, like onions, and roots, and honey, and similar things;
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	2. and I apply a mollifying ointment, if well made, and take the mucilage of vismalk, and marinate with fat of linseed or oil of silk, and apply on it;
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	3. or you take fat figs, and roast with colonic fiber, and similar medicinal things that dry the sweat;
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	There is no instance of the nodation being tightened continuously and long with wet hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And let there be movement in the limb every hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	When the tortuosity is awakened and made rigid, like a piercing, and it requires the aid of iron, if it comes close to the bone, under the subtle and light incision.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	and put on bandages and study the treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	This begins the book of dislocations.
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation comes to none, if it comes now to bring sense to the target.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if we are late, if it swells, and by chance if we put it back on the shoulder.
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	for it does not matter how we move it to the ear if it is swollen.
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	many times come to remove sand and other pains.
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	always, when this happens, if I make the patient better, then leave it, as long as the abscess is closed and relieved.
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	Then, heat the stiff and oily member, then gently reset it, and treat each member as the patient's own does.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	I have ordered the surgeons for the dislocations of the shoulder bones.
des mandibules	for the mandibles
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	There comes when the mandibles are dislocated, and there are two ways to reset them:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	Either they are a small piece of bone from their joints, and are softened a bit;
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	Or they are completely dislocated and hang downwards, and cut the saliva from the mouth that they cannot hold, nor close their mouth, and wrap their tongue with the word;
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When the dislocation is small, it returns through the more various positions.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is completely achieved and accomplished, then you must gently reset it, and do not pull hard.
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	and in such a way that the physician marks the child's head of the patient, and cuts off the nails of one of his hands at the root of the dislocation of the mandible, which is of the second part.
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	and the other hand should be cut off to make them equal.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	and instruct the patient to file his teeth and mandibles, and move them all parts.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And the surgeon makes them equal, as they should be in their place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if the head is gritty, then it is the same as the mandibles themselves, which are hot and oily, until they are reset lightly.
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	Do not try to fix the head, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	When they are returned correctly, and the patient's mouth feels well consolidated, if it is wrapped with soft cloths made of oil of rosemary and wax, then the leg is lightly tied with strings.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	And the patient sleeps on their back, and if their head is between two pillows, so that they do not move to the right or left, nor exert themselves to move, but prays lightly with lean meat, as long as the pain is steady and does not affect the jawbones.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	And then swallows what he sees lightly, and does not exert himself to open the mouth with his teeth and with drinking, as long as the jawbone is well cared for and healthy.
Et se les II mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	1. And if the two jaws cannot be set in place at once, and are not converted to their proper form, then if fevers and chills come on, and by chance the abdomen becomes distended, and by chance vomiting of clear bile occurs.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	When you see this, you will know it is a disaster.
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	And many times it has killed those who came, in nine years.
de la forcelle	3. of the force.
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	4. The force cannot be dislocated due to the cost of continuing the work and the pain, and it is always dislocated once in the defense, and it is felt by everyone.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And the restoration is that the patient stands up and holds his side with his hands.
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	and then presses the shoulder with his hand and it returns.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	then places the splint and the bandage, and tightens it.
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	and the head that is towards the cost is not able to be set.
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	if not, and if it does not dislocate at all, then reset the shoulder on his arm, as we have said.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then place the splint and bandage, and tighten it, and command the patient to rest as soon as they are able.
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	And then bring back the head of the shoulder when it is free from its socket.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	Of the shoulder dislocation
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	It is said that the shoulder is dislocated if it is not in its place according to three methods:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	that one is that it is dislocated at the part of the socket towards the side.
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	and the second is at the other end.
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	and by chance it is dislocated at the other end, and this happens rarely.
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	and do not dislocate the shoulder for the spine, and do not dislocate the tendons for the nerves.
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	and more often dislocates towards the ankle, even for those with little strength, because in this jump it is most important.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	for those with enough strength, the jump is not far, and returns to its place.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And by chance, it happens to some men that they are struck or injured, and the spine of an abscess is broken, and take care that it is not dislocated by this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	Therefore, you must check it, as long as you are certain.
et adonques encomence la cure.	and then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And it is known that dislocations occur when the shoulder is pulled towards the ankle, and there is a difference between the painful spine and the healthy one, and you will find a clear manifestation of this difference.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	You will find at the top of the shoulder a pit, and remove the covering from the top of the shoulder, just as it is with some bones.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	and the patient cannot bring their hand to their side, and make no movements.
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	And if it is dislocated above, if it is not hidden, because you can see it from the covering.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	And this manner of dislocation is not easy to reset, when it is new, or if the patient is weak.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the way is to gently lift the hand of the weak shoulder up, then remove the covering from the top, and gently release the joint at the top of the shoulder.
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	and he gently places his hand on it, extends it upwards, and then places it down.
si venra hastanment.	if help arrives.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come as we have said in our hands after, if the patient must be bathed in hot water.
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	and he applies a soothing and softening ointment, if a decoction of honey and fenugreek and honey in hot water is applied.
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	Then he wraps the patient's back with a bandage, and then puts on the other leg a stool of linen equal, not too soft or too hard, and then places the patient's foot on the stool, and gently presses the shoulder of the upper arm, and pulls the hand of the wounded one.
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	and some other signs indicate that the patient's shoulder is dislocated, if it does not move easily.
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	That shoulder is back now, and if you see if the reset is done in this way:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	and it is necessary to immediately present the patient to a surgeon who is larger than the patient.
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	and it is necessary to turn the patient to the opposite side, and pull the shoulder away from the body of the patient, and gently lift it up, so that the patient's shoulder hangs down.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	and some other signs indicate that the patient's hand is dislocated towards the abdomen.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	If the patient is too light, if there is nothing heavy for them to bear with it, then the dislocation returns now.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	1. And the resetting is also done in another way:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	2. and it is made by cutting a piece of cloth long enough to wrap around the wound, and the ends are tied together, not too tightly nor too loosely.
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	3. Then it is placed on the patient's shoulder, but if it has been too long since it was cut, and the thread is frayed, then the sling must be replaced with a new one.
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	4. Then it is extended over another hand, and the joint returns to its proper place.
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	5. If it does not return to its proper place after all these things that we have said, then this treatment is not effective.
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	1. Take the first two fingers of the left hand and three of the right, which should be able to enter through the eye socket at a point frontally on the axis, according to this form:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	2. Then tie the head of the knot with the other two fingers, so that it does not tear the patient's skin, and then place it below the patient's knee:
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	3. Extend the arm above the elbow, tie the knot with the other hand, and stretch the other arm to the elbow, then pull the hand down and leave the chest hanging from the other side:
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	The joint now reveals itself.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when it is in place, as it should be, if you happen to put the glove on the other side, then put a thread of wool even, then sprinkle powdered cinnamon with incense and almond oil all over the shoulder and the back, then pull the glove off the shoulder, turn the linen on the thread, and bind the hand on its own, and let the hands remain still.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And it is necessary that he apply a poultice as soon as the limb is comfortable, because it will heal faster.
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	and then apply more after 4 or 7 days, and move it.
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	And if it is tight and not softened, it is healthy.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint is tight due to moisture that came, or for another reason, then it is necessary that you administer cauterizations at three intervals, as it is placed before or in the chapter of cauterizations.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all this, and after 7 weeks, the joint still does not hold, and the arm cannot be raised with the elbow forward, then it is suspected that the nerve at the top of the shoulder is compressed or extended or softened.
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	And you suspect that the joint will never return to its place in the shoulder.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation that is towards the foot, and the ankles, or knees, if it is made by force, and stretching of hands, and it is treated at another time.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat as soon as it is healthy.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And after the cure comes pain in the limb, and then movement, if the patient uses cold water many times, as long as the pain is alleviated, and it returns to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	of the costly dislocation
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	The joints that are often dislocated are loosened at points, and the points return.
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	And it has become loose in all parts, and even before and after, and the dislocation is not well repaired because it can be seen and felt.
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	And it becomes loosened according to each shape.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the male member with the female, if it appears open.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	For the union is weak, and cannot grip the arm, nor touch the shoulder with anything.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And it is necessary to reset it as soon as possible, because if it is not reset as soon as possible, it would be difficult to return.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	and by chance it cannot be returned to its entirety, nevertheless when it is at the root.
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	if it is better than the others, and it causes more pain, and by chance death comes.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And the restoration if it is, when it is like this, you can bring it back with your hand to your two hands.
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	and the arms be expanded, and the hands are pulled according to the cost of the wound, from outside inward, and bind the jointure to the buttocks together, or to the root of the palm, as it revolves back to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is at the front, then it returns when he doubles his hand on his hand, and proud of the root of the palm tree that is dislocated.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	If he does not see it return to its place, then apply strong extension.
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	And if two assistants extend the arm, and hold it there, so that it does not move under extension.
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	Then turn the arm in each direction, then wrap a long and wide strip of cloth around it.
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	And when you feel the joint of the shoulder joint, if no oil has softened it, then bend the joint as much as possible, so that it does not hurt.
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	And when it is in the shoulder, if you put a dry cloth with beef grease on it against the back of the neck, and bend it as much as possible, so that it does not hurt the arm at the collar bone, and leave some fingers free, then let go.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	If the joint is tight in its place, if it loosens, and leaves it.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	If you see that the joint is not tight, if you repeat the treatment and the joint, and leave it for a while until it is firmly fixed.
puis le deslie.	Then release it.
